# Welcome | PrismAIO

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252F-MkO94f_e5GkpwEUXZga%252F-MkO9SYf4pAIbBozt6B4%252F1500x500.jpg%2520copy.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D42847701-5cd9-4f95-8e59-bae7e9b29539&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=99091f1c&sv=2)

Welcome to the PrismAIO guide collection. To get started, start by installing PrismAIO via the installation guides.

[NextAccessing and Managing](https://help.prismaio.com/online-dashboard-1/accessing-and-managing-your-license)

# Accessing and Managing | PrismAIO

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252Fuploads%252FdvZcYqyYNnHaE5L7k3aZ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8a7690fa-37c4-4b69-adc6-ce3380beb538&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ddd7d4d0&sv=2)

Accessing your license is made easy through the [dashboard](https://dashboard.prismaio.com/)
. Here, you will find everything you need to know pertaining to your PrismAIO license. Anything form multi-factor authentication to renewal is handled via the dashboard. PrismAIO **does not** use a "key" based system. Instead, we use an account based system as that provides for ultimate security and ease of use.

The same account information used to login to the dashboard is the same login information used to login to the bot.

[](https://help.prismaio.com/online-dashboard-1/accessing-and-managing-your-license#home)

Home


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252Fuploads%252F1ROmAvUq4iqNYX2sWr3F%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd52ba2c1-1a05-4011-9c55-530a3e52098c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ef647bde&sv=2)

The home tab is where you can view your expiration date and checkout statistics.

[](https://help.prismaio.com/online-dashboard-1/accessing-and-managing-your-license#settings)

**Settings**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252Fuploads%252FQ0YOanUwK27befNJbuXv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcf3d1813-829d-4efe-8b30-8a412d033042&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=33ff84c8&sv=2)

The settings tab is where you can bind your Discord, deactivate your license, and transfer your account. In addition to that, there is a security tab where you can enable two factor authentication.

[](https://help.prismaio.com/online-dashboard-1/accessing-and-managing-your-license#download)

**Download**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252Fuploads%252FpFIO0kBYo0vZkr2291F0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd238a17b-df80-4d3b-93a4-8229e699038c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a559281&sv=2)

The download tab is where you can download the latest version of PrismAIO. The dashboard will detect which operating software you are trying to download too.

[](https://help.prismaio.com/online-dashboard-1/accessing-and-managing-your-license#password-reset)

**Password Reset**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   In the event you forget the password to your account, you can reset your password via [https://dashboard.prismaio.com/reset-password](https://dashboard.prismaio.com/reset-password)
    

[PreviousWelcome](https://help.prismaio.com/)
[NextRenewal](https://help.prismaio.com/online-dashboard-1/renewing-account)

# Renewal | PrismAIO

[](https://help.prismaio.com/online-dashboard-1/renewing-account#pricing)

Pricing


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   $50 every month, starting from the purchase date and can be renewed via the [dashboard](https://dashboard.prismaio.com/)
    .
    

*   PrismAIO can be renewed at anytime. Accounts are **never** deleted/destroyed.
    
*   Failure to renew within 2-weeks after your expiration date will result in the renewal price increasing to $300 for the first billing cycle.
    

[](https://help.prismaio.com/online-dashboard-1/renewing-account#faq)

FAQ


------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   PrismAIO can be renewed at any time. Once renewed, an additional 1 month will be added to the current expiration date. If you choose not to renew, your account will **not** be destroyed meaning you can renew at any point in the future. However, after a 1 day grace period, you will lose access to the bot and Discord. In order to regain access back to these, you must renew.
    
*   All payment processing is handled by Stripe and we do not store any information.
    

[PreviousAccessing and Managing](https://help.prismaio.com/online-dashboard-1/accessing-and-managing-your-license)
[NextTwo Factor Authentication](https://help.prismaio.com/online-dashboard-1/two-factor-authentication)

Last updated 3 years ago

Was this helpful?

# Transferring Account | PrismAIO

[](https://help.prismaio.com/online-dashboard-1/transferring-account#transferring-account)

Transferring Account


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Transferring account will transfer your PrismAIO license from your account and remove you from the discord.
    

To transfer your account, press the `Request` button that corresponds to the `Account Transfer` column.

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252Fuploads%252FwdpYtPmcC53ptgFMv96Q%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5b519a79-b54b-4e19-9476-a09fa33b371f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f3147d5&sv=2)

This will open a popup where you can input the email that belongs to the account you want to transfer to.

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252Fuploads%252FWCJGDFCsgi8RXx3A0JJG%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd2051809-4231-4248-9fb6-913b5df3ac6a&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=13c5a075&sv=2)

Press "Transfer." If you have two-factor authentication enabled, you will have to complete that as well.

**The email you put in must belong to an account.** If no account exists for the email you want to transfer to, please sign up at [https://prismaio.com/signup](https://prismaio.com/signup)
.

Both you and the recipient will receive an email with a link that you have to press in order to confirm the transfer.

[![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F165490796%2Fd8f1875d6700b0b69ff56cff%2FScreen%2BShot%2B2019-11-24%2Bat%2B2.44.10%2BPM.png%3Fexpires%3D1620781200%26signature%3Dd29c1755d099b73e43bf1bf9602b63daaccfd61a2a38d96dc4df7c5154393273&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bf93e4a5&sv=2)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/165490796/d8f1875d6700b0b69ff56cff/Screen+Shot+2019-11-24+at+2.44.10+PM.png?expires=1620781200&signature=d29c1755d099b73e43bf1bf9602b63daaccfd61a2a38d96dc4df7c5154393273)

After both you and the recipient click the link, the transfer will be complete.

[](https://help.prismaio.com/online-dashboard-1/transferring-account#faq)

**F.A.Q:**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

What does "User transfer not found mean"?

*   This error means that you are trying to transfer to an email that is not an active Prism account. If you are getting this error, please create an account at [https://dashboard.prismaio.com/signup](https://dashboard.prismaio.com/signup)
     and try the transfer again.
    

Why can't I transfer my account (Account not transferable)?

*   If you purchased from a restock or groupbuy, accounts are not allowed to be transferred for 3 months.
    

[PreviousTwo Factor Authentication](https://help.prismaio.com/online-dashboard-1/two-factor-authentication)
[NextSelling on BotBroker](https://help.prismaio.com/online-dashboard-1/transferring-account/selling-on-botbroker)

# Two Factor Authentication | PrismAIO

[](https://help.prismaio.com/online-dashboard-1/two-factor-authentication#app-setup)

App Setup


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/online-dashboard-1/two-factor-authentication#step-1)

**Step 1:**

*   Download Google Authenticator via the Apple App Store or Google Play Store.
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F200949407%2F3dd2131c89301d1ca47cf7c0%2Fgoogle%2Bauth2.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c8f8db48&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/online-dashboard-1/two-factor-authentication#step-2)

**Step 2:**

*   Upon opening the app for the first time, you should see a "BEGIN SETUP" button at the bottom of the screen. Click on that so you will be presented with a "scan barcode" and "manual entry" button. Click on the "scan barcode" option.
    

#### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/online-dashboard-1/two-factor-authentication#step-3)

**Step 3:**

*   After setting up the app, head over to the [dashboard](https://www.prismaio.com/dashboard)
    . Once signed in, you will see a "Two Factor" tab. In that tab, you will see a green "Enable" button. Next to that button, there is a "Link MFA" button. Click on that button.
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F201324469%2Fa2e1a2c73decde8ebe9e89bf%2Fmfa%2Btab.PNG&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=31ac5d3a&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/online-dashboard-1/two-factor-authentication#step-4)

**Step 4:**

*   Once you click that button, you will be presented with a pop-up link MFA window. Click on the "Request QR Code" where a new tab will open containing your unique QR code.
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F201324611%2Ffa9b0f4d336651324bb4d1d3%2FFull%2BMFA%2Btba.PNG&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=70fca1e3&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/online-dashboard-1/two-factor-authentication#step-5)

**Step 5:**

For new Google Authenticator:

*   Use the "scan barcode" option in setup to scan the barcode.
    

For existing Google Authenticator Users:

*   With the barcode open, head back to Google Authenticator and click on the + button in the top right-hand corner. Now head to the bottom of that screen and click on "Scan Barcode." Scan the barcode that the dashboard opened in your web-browser.
    

For everyone:

*   Upon a successful scan, you will than see a new tab in the app that contains a 6-digit combination. Use that combination to fill in the "Code" section in the dashboard. Upon a successful combination, you will see the "Link MFA" change to "Unlink MFA" in the dashboard.
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F201324432%2Fa540c1856847be1626d5531c%2Fcode%2Bmfa.PNG&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6ffef526&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/online-dashboard-1/two-factor-authentication#step-6)

**Step 6:**

*   Click on the green "Enable" button. If everything went well, you will see a text file download which contains very important backup codes. In the event you get locked out, these codes will allow you to bypass using your phone or authentication app. You can regenerate these codes at any time by clicking the "Generate" button in the backup codes section.
    

Make sure you save your backup codes in a safe and easily accessible place!

[](https://help.prismaio.com/online-dashboard-1/two-factor-authentication#sms)

**SMS**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/online-dashboard-1/two-factor-authentication#step-1-1)

**Step 1:**

*   Make sure you have enable Two Factor via the [dashboard](https://www.prismaio.com/dashboard)
    .
    

#### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/online-dashboard-1/two-factor-authentication#step-2-1)

**Step 2:**

*   Click on the "Link Phone" button in the Phone tab.
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F201328026%2Ff1881179bff25ba2da1ff699%2FPhone%2BTab.PNG&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e9dd574b&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/online-dashboard-1/two-factor-authentication#step-3-1)

**Step 3:**

*   Type in your phone number into the box and click request code.
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F201328411%2F09b54d5c849ed4b30e6d1ca8%2Fphone%2Btab%2B2.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7bec0c&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/online-dashboard-1/two-factor-authentication#step-4-1)

**Step 4:**

*   Type the code sent to your phone into the "Code" box and click submit.
    
*   After that, you phone can now be used to receive your authentication codes!
    

[PreviousRenewal](https://help.prismaio.com/online-dashboard-1/renewing-account)
[NextTransferring Account](https://help.prismaio.com/online-dashboard-1/transferring-account)

# Proxies | PrismAIO

*   Proxies are used to mask your IP address to allow you to run multiple tasks without getting your IP banned
    

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/proxies#adding--managing-proxies)

Adding + Managing Proxies


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Proxies can be created and managed by navigating to the proxy tab.
    
*   To create a new list, first name your proxy list and then paste your proxies into the `proxies` section
    

Each proxy must be on it's own line (one proxy per line)

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252F-MkCyew942MsG3eNvvN9%252F-MkCzRIC0irR7rXOifn6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D23a5c049-8ae8-4726-91ce-0987fc73b654&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e62a1f32&sv=2)

[PreviousProfiles](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/profiles)
[NextSettings](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/settings)

Last updated 4 years ago

# Delays | PrismAIO

*   When creating tasks, there are two different delays to add: monitor delay and task delay
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/delays#monitor-delay)

Monitor Delay

*   The monitor delay is the delay by which the monitor threads will monitor for the product. A lower monitor delay will result in faster product pickup times.
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252F-MkTfAXreFhwY_MoglIs%252F-MkTgZ1AjziQoDn1NM5M%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc13e9b7c-5c18-4c62-9ce6-633937bc5255&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bf2496ff&sv=2)

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/delays#task-delay)

Task Delay

*   The task delay is the delay by which the task will try and add a product to cart.
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252F-MkTfAXreFhwY_MoglIs%252F-MkTgqxOaNgDxVAeT3HO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4fea98e0-792c-4506-861b-b08fc95531b5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=12fe67d5&sv=2)

Both delays are required. Be careful as too low delays will result in proxy/IP bans

[PreviousTask Creation](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/task-creation)
[NextProfiles](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/profiles)

Last updated 4 years ago

# Uninstall | PrismAIO

*   Uninstalling will permanently delete all of your data in the bot. If done correctly, you will be starting fresh.
    

Start Here

[](https://help.prismaio.com/installation/uninstall#tab-start-here)

Windows

[](https://help.prismaio.com/installation/uninstall#tab-windows)

Mac

[](https://help.prismaio.com/installation/uninstall#tab-mac)

*   Click the tab corresponding to the device you are reinstalling PrismAIO on.
    

1.  Go to your Windows settings page and click on the systems option.
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F206060802%2F0e9eed474f03461929e32b03%2Funinstall%2B1.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c41ded8&sv=2)

2\. Click on the "Apps and Features" tab and locate the PrismAIO application. Click uninstall.

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F206061202%2F828f661c999feb8658fb5734%2Fprism%2Buninstall%2Bpic%2B1.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5cacf778&sv=2)

3\. Then go to your desktop and click CTRL + R on your keyboard to open the run window. Type into the box: `%appdata%` and press OK.

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F206061733%2F34889c4c7ae0490109e2ac50%2Frun%2Bwindow.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=eb2c0a1a&sv=2)

4\. Scroll down and locate the PrismAIO folder. Right click the folder and click delete.

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F206064419%2F8a2cdb8cbe527b957722bd83%2Freplacement.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=93b56b1d&sv=2)

5\. Then click on the `AppData` folder up top. You should see the Local, LocalLow, and Roaming folder. Click the Local folder and locate the `prismaio-updater` folder. Right click the folder and press delete.

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F206063355%2F06c62a398e336f87ae9e94b2%2Fclick.png&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e539e9db&sv=2)![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F206063422%2Fe3a511b9356f2414dbc30f90%2Fimage.png&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=419e91d9&sv=2)![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F206063857%2F127889433c7c3bc2f82d32c8%2Fimage.png&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bb1373ee&sv=2)

6\. You are now ready to do a fresh install from the dashboard. For best performance, we suggest you restart your system before re-installing. When you are ready to re-install, please log into the dashboard and choose the windows icon below to re-install.

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F206065032%2F67e9bd7ad1dd6af1ef0e62b6%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a2a969cd&sv=2)

1.  Navigate to finder and once you are in finder, move your cursor all the way to the top of your computer and find `"Go"` and click on it.
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F232956864%2Fec98633f466b1948ae580c3b%2FScreen%2BShot%2B2020-08-03%2Bat%2B1.30.37%2BPM.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2403186b&sv=2)

2\. While in the go menu, hold the `"Option"` key to reveal a folder called `"Library"`

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F232958962%2Ff18f7d38dd94e013d33f5310%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8930ba83&sv=2)

3\. Navigate to the `"Application Support"` and than to `"PrismAIO"`

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F232959874%2Ffebab2dc9c428da1dc1dc355%2FScreen%2BShot%2B2020-08-03%2Bat%2B1.39.22%2BPM.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fe2d795f&sv=2)

4\. Right click the `"PrismAIO"` and click `"Move To Trash"`![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F232960138%2Fa186f7deaedeeb8aa260eafe%2FScreen%2BShot%2B2020-08-03%2Bat%2B1.40.43%2BPM.png&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f9e4c64d&sv=2)

5\. After moving that folder to the trash, you can proceed by re-downloading via the [dashboard](https://dashboard.prismaio.com/)
.

# Selling on BotBroker | PrismAIO

Bot Broker is the safest and easiest way to sell Prism. They provide a seamless transaction that protects both the buyer and seller. Selling on BotBroker is easy!

#### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/online-dashboard-1/transferring-account/selling-on-botbroker#step-1)

**Step 1:**

*   Signup for their site via [https://botbroker.io/signup](https://botbroker.io/signup)
    .
    

#### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/online-dashboard-1/transferring-account/selling-on-botbroker#step-2)

**Step 2:**

*   Head over to the [Prism page](https://botbroker.io/products/prism)
    .
    

#### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/online-dashboard-1/transferring-account/selling-on-botbroker#step-3)

**Step 3:**

*   Scroll down until you are presented with the asks and bids. To sell PrismAIO, click on place an ask where you will then be directed to the [sell page](https://botbroker.io/products/prism)
    .
    

#### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/online-dashboard-1/transferring-account/selling-on-botbroker#step-4)

**Step 4:**

*   As PrismAIO uses a set of login credentials vs. a key, a request token is needed for BotBroker. To get this code, head over to the [dashboard](https://dashboard.prismaio.com/)
    . Once there, find BotBroker section, as shown below:
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252Fuploads%252FtnF0ha7RiqXha4LE6g2N%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D71cf4539-1b14-4a96-90a9-2c7678eb0e38&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=685a9e81&sv=2)

Than click on the red "Request" button where you will be sent an email containing the code.

[![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F200666701%2Fa10d804b61701f1d41e44182%2Fprism%2Bbb%2Btoken.jpg&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5f5d7cff&sv=2)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/200666701/a10d804b61701f1d41e44182/prism+bb+token.jpg)

#### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/online-dashboard-1/transferring-account/selling-on-botbroker#step-5)

**Step 5:**

*   Copy that code and paste it in the key section on the listing page on BotBroker. Fill out the remaining information and confirm the listing!
    

[PreviousTransferring Account](https://help.prismaio.com/online-dashboard-1/transferring-account)
[NextInstall](https://help.prismaio.com/installation/install)

# Dashboard Analytics | PrismAIO

Here, you can view your recent checkouts and watch your checkout graph climb with every item you hit. On the analytics section, you will see a way to sort your checkouts by day (d), week (w), month (m), and year (y). There is also a cumulative toggle that will show your success in a cumulative fashion.

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252F-Mk007vNolgbl2QFg0DG%252F-Mk00hqIqtAA8ncpVAqG%252Fupdated%2520prism%2520dash.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dabe128b8-0ea1-4133-b7a2-f886ed614741&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3a3faa8b&sv=2)

# Release Calendar | PrismAIO

Located on the dashboard tab inside the bot, you will see a "Weekly Release Calendar" section. The release calendar is where you can find upcoming releases and create tasks for those releases with just a few clicks.

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/in-bot-dashboard/release-calendar#using-the-release-calendar)

Using the Release Calendar

1.  Locate the date of the release and click on it.
    
2.  If the release has been added to the bot, you will see a photo and name of the release.
    
3.  Once you have located the item you want to attempt to go for, click on "See Details"
    
4.  Upon clicking it, you will see a window open that includes all the supported releases of the item. You will also see the time of the release which is based on your local time.
    
5.  Next, choose the site(s) you want to run PrismAIO on. Click on the "Create Group" button which will automatically create a group with the suggested monitor input, along with prompting you to create your tasks. If you choose not to create your tasks in that window, you can click the "View" button which will take you directly to the newly created task group.
    

Releases are updated at the beginning of every month. If a release is not there, rest assured it will be added to the calendar.

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252F-Mk00njadnrR2lsf8imf%252F-Mk00sLT2Gp8GcX_7AoL%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2d2be47f-0dc8-4b7d-9a8b-b5d55dc7545e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f40e84fe&sv=2)

[PreviousDashboard Analytics](https://help.prismaio.com/in-bot-dashboard/dashboard-analytics)
[NextTask Creation](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/task-creation)

# Install | PrismAIO

*   Head on over to the [dashboard](https://dashboard.prismaio.com/)
     to download
    

**System Requirements:**

*   Memory (RAM)**:** `4 GB`
    
*   Disk Space: `5 GB`
    

Start Here

[](https://help.prismaio.com/installation/install#tab-start-here)

Windows

[](https://help.prismaio.com/installation/install#tab-windows)

Mac

[](https://help.prismaio.com/installation/install#tab-mac)

*   Click the tab corresponding to the device you are installing PrismAIO on.
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/installation/install#step-1)

**Step 1:**

Click the button below to download the Windows version

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252Fuploads%252FhAHtw7pYYjNBr3Bn7mNr%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D84c1618b-932a-423a-b243-806a4a0fa873&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2297c0c9&sv=2)

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/installation/install#step-2)

**Step 2:**

*   Click the `prism-setup.exe` folder to get started. This can be found by heading to `file explorer -> downloads` and double-clicking the Prism download file.
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/installation/install#step-3)

Step 3:

*   Proceed with the setup by following the on-screen instructions.
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/installation/install#step-4)

Step 4:

*   Login using the **same email and password that you use to login to the dashboard.** If everything is correct, PrismAIO will open and you will be presented with the bot.
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252F-MjplEvzUyF8dSpFv3DR%252F-Mjpo8yhPVzmBWqKuvdX%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df94f3f4e-f997-4f53-90d7-4bdb2441c12d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6093037b&sv=2)

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/installation/install#step-1-1)

**Step 1:**

Click the corresponding button below to download the Mac version

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252Fuploads%252Fy5g0jBuAiWunoidRrh8T%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D012af670-8a07-41da-bf14-f1593e973247&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7e44f064&sv=2)

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/installation/install#step-2-1)

**Step 2:**

*   Go ahead and click the `prism-setup.dmg` file to get started. This can be found my heading to `Finder -> Downloads` and double-clicking the Prism download.
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/installation/install#step-3-1)

Step 3:

*   Drag the PrismAIO icon into the Applications folder. Then, double click the PrismAIO application to open.
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/installation/install#step-4-1)

Step 4:

*   Login using the **same email and password that you use to login to the dashboard.** If everything is correct, PrismAIO will open and you will be presented with the bot.
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252F-MjplEvzUyF8dSpFv3DR%252F-Mjpo8yhPVzmBWqKuvdX%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df94f3f4e-f997-4f53-90d7-4bdb2441c12d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6093037b&sv=2)

# Profiles | PrismAIO

*   The billing page can be accessed by clicking the profile option on the left-hand task bar.
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252F-MkAB98Su6ht8ucBMZWM%252F-MkABdzBM36jBqh8Kuv0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7525853f-4f3e-4db8-b53d-23fb963baccf&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8c42b92c&sv=2)

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/profiles#creation)

Creation


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   To create a billing profile, press the `+` button near the top icons and a pop-up will appear.
    

#### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/profiles#undefined)

#### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/profiles#general-tab)

General Tab

*   The general tab is where general profile information will go.
    

Profile Name

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/profiles#tab-profile-name)

Email

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/profiles#tab-email)

Cardholder Name

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/profiles#tab-cardholder-name)

Card Number

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/profiles#tab-card-number)

CVV

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/profiles#tab-cvv)

Month EXP.

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/profiles#tab-month-exp)

Year EXP.

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/profiles#tab-year-exp)

*   Type in any name in to this box. We recommend you choose something that helps you identify which profile to use when creating tasks.
    

*   Enter in any email. We recommend have a unique email for each profile.
    

*   We recommend you use the name shown on your credit card/account.
    

*   Enter in your credit card number.
    

*   This value is typically found on the back of your credit card and is usually three digits. If you have an American Express card, this is found on the front of your card and is four digits.
    

*   This is shorthand for expiration month. Choose the month from the drop down options.
    

*   This is shorthand for expiration year. Choose the year from the drop down options.
    

#### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/profiles#shipping-tab)

Shipping Tab

*   The shipping tab is where shipping information will go.
    

First Name

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/profiles#tab-first-name)

Last Name

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/profiles#tab-last-name)

Address

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/profiles#tab-address)

Address 2

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/profiles#tab-address-2)

City

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/profiles#tab-city)

Phone

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/profiles#tab-phone)

Country

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/profiles#tab-country)

State

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/profiles#tab-state)

Postal Code

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/profiles#tab-postal-code)

*   Enter in your first name.
    

*   Enter in your last name.
    

*   Enter in your main address line.
    

*   Enter in your apartment, suite, etc.
    

*   Enter in your city name.
    

*   Enter in your phone number. Make sure that your number is correctly formatted in your country code.
    

*   Select one of the countries from the drop down list.
    

*   Select one of the states from the drop down list.
    

*   Enter in your postal code. If you have a space in your zip code, include it as way.
    

**Billing Tab**

*   This tab is where the billing address will go. If it is the same address as the shipping address, enable, `Same As Shipping.`
    

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/profiles#profile-groups)

Profile Groups


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Profile groups are designed to make it easier to mass select profiles.
    

#### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/profiles#creation-1)

Creation

*   To create a profile group, click `Groups` in the top-right corner of the billing/profile page.
    
*   To create a new group, click `Create`.
    
*   Once there, select the profiles you want to add my holding `ctrl + click` or `shift + click`
    
*   Lastly, name the group and click create.
    

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/profiles#import-export)

Import/Export


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Profiles can be imported and exported by clicking either of these buttons at the top of the billing/profile page. The left icon is to import, the right icon is to export.
    

Profiles must be converted to Prism format prior to being imported.

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252F-MkCwk6ghe9rvt0JzRiy%252F-MkCyLoZnUux1HsDltSH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D72ec5b76-6cdf-414b-9d31-c3aa9b461850&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a6570f1&sv=2)

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/profiles#faq)

FAQ


-------------------------------------------------------------------------

How many profiles do I need?

*   Ideally each task will have a unique profile.
    

How should I jig my profile?

*   Please refer to your cook group on how to properly jig.

# Automations | PrismAIO

The automations tab allows for 24/7 monitoring of products without the risk of banning your proxies. Automations works by using our monitors to monitor products and if the monitors pickup a product that matches your inputted keywords or PID, your tasks will automatically be created and started.

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/automations#setup)

Setup


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Before setting up automations, make sure all of your quick task settings in "Site Options" are filled in. This ensures that your tasks will function properly when running for sites other then footsites.

Start by navigating to the automations tab.

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252F-Mk-uSuLKudtKe7BXEkr%252F-Mk-utp1b_e3kIiidPEN%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D524be00d-105d-48de-9e33-b1f3c108965a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bb861116&sv=2)

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/automations#general-section)

**General Section**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/automations#monitor-inputs)

**Monitor Inputs**

This is where you want to put the products you want to monitor for. Whether it be PIDs or keywords, this section covers both. You are allowed one monitor input per line (similar to variants). Follow the tabs below on properly formatting monitor inputs.

PID

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/automations#tab-pid)

Keywords

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/automations#tab-keywords)

Links

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/automations#tab-links)

Variants

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/automations#tab-variants)

C4991004 C4991500 4991101M 75441201

(+yeezy,+foam,+ochre) (+dunk,+low,+championship,-gs,-ps,-td,-grade,-pre,-kids) (+dunk,+low,+university,+red,+white,+total,+orange,-gs,-ps,-td,-grade,-pre,-kids)

https://kith.com/products/aagw3354 https://kith.com/products/JB414571-144 https://kith.com/products/JBDJ3003-144

41097797501134

41097797533902

41097797566670

41097797599438

41097797632206

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/automations#automation-section)

**Automation Section**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/automations#starting-and-stopping)

**Starting & Stopping**

There are four parameters for starting tasks via automations. Only one parameter has to be checked, but you can enable multiple depending on the site.

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252Fuploads%252FML38O6cy7y0313E1UtNO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D018b01fd-4f99-48a0-a831-0d5309267180&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=273b3068&sv=2)

`Start on monitor (Shopify):` starts tasks as soon as Prism's third-party monitor pings.

`Start on checkpoint (Shopify):` starts tasks as soon as Prism's third-party monitor pings that checkpoint on the site you are running goes up.

*   `Stop when checkpoint goes down (Shopify):` stops tasks when checkpoint is disabled on a site regardless of if the product dropped or not.
    
    *   `Create one empty group:` create ONE task group with no monitor input when checkpoint goes up which allows you to mass link change to the product that dropped.
        
    *   `Create one group per link:` creates one task group PER link in your automation group.
        
        *   Depending on how many links you have, this can create a lot of tasks that can quickly become too many to manage so be careful!
            
        
    

`Start on checkouts:` starts tasks after Prism's checkouts surpass your set number of checkouts

`Start on carts:` starts tasks after Prism carts your set number globally.

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/automations#site-selection)

Site Selection

*   You can choose to monitor only a select few sites or all sites at once. Be careful with your keywords/monitor inputs if using all sites as you don't want to pickup the wrong product.
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252F-Mk-uSuLKudtKe7BXEkr%252F-Mk-yztEzUi4pbs-tIAO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D624aab9e-9000-464b-929d-a735945f2325&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5113d9ca&sv=2)

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/automations#task-data-section)

Task Data Section


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Under this section, choose your sizes, profiles or profile groups, proxy list, and task quantity per profile.
    

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/automations#monitor-pop-out)

Monitor Pop Out


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   The monitor pop-out is a quick and easy way to watch the Prism checkout logs, as well as the monitors. To access the monitor pop-out, click the "Monitor" button near the top-right of Prism.
    

**Checkout Feed:** The checkout feed consists of Prism's checkout log and is updated in real time

**Monitor:** The monitor section consists of the unfiltered shopify section and is also updated in real time.

**Quick Tasks:**

*   In both the checkout feed and monitor section, there is a size option and paperclip option. Clicking the size will create a quick task, clicking the paperclip will copy the URL of the product to the clipboard.
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252F-Mk-uSuLKudtKe7BXEkr%252F-Mk0-BzLbur5EhndvAQh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da16ff04f-f44b-4f2e-98cb-1209e1bd8266&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a5fe4712&sv=2)

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/automations#suggested-setups)

Suggested Setups


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/automations#footsites)

Footsites

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252Fuploads%252FpxfiQXW2qQRixbZZS8qY%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D01f73091-2640-4708-9356-e9bd34513aa7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bae3f3e0&sv=2)

*   Suggested SKU list can be found [here](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/footsites-north-america/automation-sku-list)
    .
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/automations#shopify)

Shopify

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252Fuploads%252Fk6wrBge5R2JCenYjArUj%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7d72649b-7d55-47e4-a9f7-741c31ee1b1d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=84973077&sv=2)

Note: you can change checkpoint start setting depending on how you want your tasks to be created.

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/automations#webhook)

Webhook


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   To get notifications for automation start and stops, add a webhook to the `Notification` webhook spot in the settings tab.
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252Fuploads%252FRQQI5U49olc1hU0KvioR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dba85e3e1-f5ca-449d-9d46-92b1a0091fe0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=80e3abb5&sv=2)

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/automations#faq)

FAQ


----------------------------------------------------------------------------

What products can I monitor?

*   You can monitor PIDs, keywords, and links (for sites that support it). You cannot monitor variants for a product.
    

How many products can I monitor?

*   You can monitor as many products as you want to.
    

Will my data be used when using automations?

*   Your data will only be used once tasks start.
    

Can I use gift cards for footsites?

*   Yes. Select your gift card list in site options and automations will automatically use it.
    

Can I change my captcha source?

*   Yes. Select which captcha source you want in site options and automations will automatically use it.

# Gift Cards | PrismAIO

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/footsites-north-america/gift-cards#purchasing-gift-cards)

**Purchasing Gift Cards**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   In order to add gift cards to the bot, you must purchase them. The best place to order gift cards is directly from their website which can be found [here](https://www.footlocker.com/product/giftcard/ECARD21.html)
    .
    

In order for the gift card function to be utilized correctly, you should have enough balance to cover an entire pair of shoes.

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/footsites-north-america/gift-cards#adding-gift-cards-to-the-bot)

**Adding Gift Cards to the Bot**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   After you have purchased your gift cards, head over to the settings tab in the bot. Once there, you will see a tab called "Gift Cards"
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F325193121%2F078dedba21482a5a791f18a3%2Fimage.png%3Fexpires%3D1619722410%26signature%3D5a4cf0a6248c1f863d993052c77c810499af78806cf8a73f62c642d63aa81aa0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=72e23466&sv=2)

*   Once there, you will see the gift card hub where you can manage your gift card lists and check your balances.
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252F-MkT5DmDkPkYOLf6Toos%252F-MkTNyyYo4CraklTNJsN%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7e3ad460-d101-41b3-8517-77452b3e6ed7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d4e3dd41&sv=2)

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/footsites-north-america/gift-cards#h_42b3ba13d6-1)

**Creating a Gift Card List**

*   A gift card list can be created by choosing a name, assigning a site, and adding your cards. Card are added in `card:pin:balance` format. For example, if your card # is `6199111111119510` and your online pin # is `12345678`, you would add it to the bot as `6199111111119510:12345678`. If you don't want to check the balance, you can manually add it by adding the balance to the end of the `card:pin`combination. Each card and pin combo must be on its own line. Once you have your cards added, click the create button. A completed list is shown below.
    
*   If you click the `$` sign, the bot will check the balance left on the giftcard. By clicking `Balances`, it will pull the balance for all your gift cards.
    

You **must** check your balance or add a balance manually for gift cards to work properly.

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252F-MkT5DmDkPkYOLf6Toos%252F-MkTOiRcNRhyvp0JLJot%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3ae9c649-8fad-4370-8add-8d9c77aab969&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e4745ef8&sv=2)

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/footsites-north-america/gift-cards#assigning-to-tasks)

**Assigning to Tasks**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F325819843%2F1f28e42ad02dd03654497259%2Fimage.png%3Fexpires%3D1619722410%26signature%3Dff53c80f799ca4bba54728ea61b42d4af3d6dbf2a39cf4872cf671bf47d3aa94&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cdc3238e&sv=2)

*   When creating tasks, you will see a gift card list section. Choose whichever gift card list you want to run.
    

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/footsites-north-america/gift-cards#faq)

**FAQ**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

How many giftcards do I need?

*   Unfortunately, there is no way to give a specific answer as it changes from user to user and from release to release. We recommend having enough in giftcards to cover your past release success as that can be a good indication on how you might preform on upcoming drops.
    

Can I use the same giftcard or giftcard list on all footsites?

*   Yes.
    

What happens if I run out of giftcards?

*   If the gift card cannot cover the entire purchase, the bot will use whatever amount is left on the gift card and will then cover the rest with the profile assigned to the task.
    

Do I need to check the balance?

*   Yes!
    

[](https://successbyjack.gitbook.io/prism-test/footsites-north-america/misc.-guides/flx-accounts)

[PreviousFootsites (USA) Automation SKU List](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/footsites-north-america/automation-sku-list)
[NextFLX Accounts](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/footsites-north-america/flx-accounts)

# Raffle Entry | PrismAIO

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/footsites-north-america/raffle-entry#task-creation)

Task Creation


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Before creating tasks, you must create a new task group for the footsite **raffle** you want to run on. For help on creating a new task group, follow [this guide.](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/task-creation)
    
    *   Your options are: `Foot Locker Raffle, Champs Raffle,`and `Kids Foot Locker Raffle`
        
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/footsites-north-america/raffle-entry#monitor-setup)

Monitor Setup

*   **Product ID:** use the product PID provided by our release guides, via a third-party, of on their site. Using a direct link will not work.
    
*   **Proxy List:** used for monitoring only. Can be the same as your task list.
    
*   **Delay:** monitor delay. Recommended to be left at `5000`
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/footsites-north-america/raffle-entry#captcha-settings)

Captcha Settings

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252Fuploads%252FNPy6gxs5466SUbvN5imf%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dba0024e0-9227-441b-87cc-380c8cdc81ab&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ad9f018e&sv=2)

*   You do not need captcha for raffles - just leave captcha settings at default.
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/footsites-north-america/raffle-entry#task-creation-1)

Task Creation

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252Fuploads%252FC0uYY1wgC1qfHWRFsKZl%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D59f96393-7154-4768-8c71-97b25986d71f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5d192a2d&sv=2)

Required Fields

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/footsites-north-america/raffle-entry#tab-required-fields)

Optional Fields

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/footsites-north-america/raffle-entry#tab-optional-fields)

*   **Profiles:** choose your profiles/profile group
    
*   **Account:** choose the accounts you want to enter on
    
*   **In-store Raffle:** enable if you want tasks to enter for in-store near the zip code on your profile
    
*   **Delay:** task delay. Recommended to be left at `5000`
    
*   **Proxy List:** proxy list used to checkout (leave blank for localhost)
    
*   **Size:** size(s) the task will go for. If selecting multiple sizes, it will go for any size in your range.
    

*   **Gift Card List:** Gift card list the tasks will use
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/footsites-north-america/raffle-entry#head-starts)

Head Starts

*   Head starts can be obtained by redeeming FLX points on the account. Each head start costs 500 points, typically with a max of 3 head starts per account. To add head starts when entering your accounts, enter the number of head start you want to add. If you want to use max head starts, enable the `Use Max Head Starts` toggle.
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252Fuploads%252F2q2ZK9pHhBfOODS2e3th%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3d08aab7-2ec3-4aaf-a9a2-dd2ce27214a5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5c7a4c61&sv=2)

If using max head starts and your account does not have enough points to max out boots, it will add as many boosts as it can. For example: it costs 1500 points for three boosts, but your account only has 1250 boots, if using max head starts PrismAIO will add two boots to your entry.

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/footsites-north-america/raffle-entry#faq)

FAQ


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Why are my tasks stuck "Submitting Raffle"?

*   Their site struggles very badly when entering the raffle. Just let all your tasks run and it will eventually go through.
    

What does "Session Expired" mean?

*   This is normal. Just let your tasks run.
    

How many accounts do I need?

*   The more the better.
    

How many profiles do I need?

*   Each account should have a unique profile.
    

Do I need unique information on each profile?

*   Yes
    

Can I enter all footsites on the same account?

*   Yes
    

Do my accounts need to have information already saved on them?

*   No. If PrismAIO detects the account has no information saved, it will save the info on your profile to that account. If it has information already saved on the account, it will use that to enter.
    

[PreviousMulti SKU Monitoring](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/footsites-north-america/multi-sku-monitoring)
[NextShopify](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify)

Last updated 2 years ago

Was this helpful?

# Multi SKU Monitoring | PrismAIO

Multi SKU monitoring allows you to mass-monitor footsite products using your own monitor proxy and data. Unlike Automations, multi SKU monitoring will require users to use their proxies to monitor products. This is best utilized for those who want the fastest possible pickup time and can afford the data consumption and amount of ISP proxies necessary. **Only works on restocks.**

Multi SKU monitoring is for **footsites only**

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/footsites-north-america/multi-sku-monitoring#setup)

Setup


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Multi SKU can be enabled by heading to task group settings and clicking `Enable Multi SKU`
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252Fuploads%252Fp0SDM8eUNVZPYwOwlFrl%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Def441463-b93d-4121-9daf-4a2fba419c60&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=96f7c9d1&sv=2)

From there, you can now add multiple SKUs to the monitor input box

Only one SKU per line

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252Fuploads%252FI70zepBNWFWuW0Nhl9tK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D96c1bb97-78c2-4e50-a531-4d55f678d7b2&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4e99a9cf&sv=2)

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/footsites-north-america/multi-sku-monitoring#faq)

FAQ


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Do I need proxies?

*   Yes! Multi SKU will use your monitor proxies to monitor for products.
    

How many proxies do I need?

*   2+ proxies per SKU being monitored
    

Does it use my monitor proxy data?

*   Yes. It is recommended to only monitor with ISP/DC or unmetered proxies. Task data is not used until a product is picked up.
    

What happens if it picks up two products at the same time?

*   If two or more products pickup at the same time, the bot will go for whichever product is picked up first. After that product is sold out or if tasks are rotating `Out of Stock, retrying...`, it will randomly go to another product that you are monitoring for that is still in-stock. If no product is in-stock, tasks will go back to `Waiting for Product/Restock`
    

Should I use this on initial drop?

No. Multi SKU is meant for restocks. Never use it on initial drop.

[PreviousFLX Accounts](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/footsites-north-america/flx-accounts)
[NextRaffle Entry](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/footsites-north-america/raffle-entry)

Last updated 2 years ago

Was this helpful?

# FLX Accounts | PrismAIO

Here are the positives of using accounts:

*   Free shipping for FLX account members
    
*   Ability to accumulate points in your FLX account which can later be used for in-store reservation boosts etc
    
*   Less likely to trigger Payment Verification emails (unconfirmed)
    

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/footsites-north-america/flx-accounts#setup)

**S**etup:


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252F-MkT5DmDkPkYOLf6Toos%252F-MkTNbQHB1jwgDWU2qwi%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df628f100-8751-4db5-a972-9fab48c330b1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b55aff98&sv=2)

*   Specific accounts and account groups can be selected when creating footsite tasks.
    

**It is important to note that you can only use ONE ACCOUNT PER TASK!** If you use the same account across multiple tasks, the account will be disabled permanently.

[PreviousGift Cards](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/footsites-north-america/gift-cards)
[NextMulti SKU Monitoring](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/footsites-north-america/multi-sku-monitoring)

Last updated 4 years ago

Was this helpful?

# Task Creation | PrismAIO

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/task-creation#task-group-creation)

Task Group Creation


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Before creating tasks, a task group must first be created. To create a task group, navigate to the `Tasks Groups` section and click `New Task Group +`
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252F-MkNCarF99XonymaF_uX%252F-MkNMYAN6ogQb8MFaJx-%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da22831e0-b53e-4d49-aef8-77501c043493&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=520c017&sv=2)

*   From there, name your group and choose the site you want to run on.
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252F-MkNCarF99XonymaF_uX%252F-MkNMptPj77uVA99yNtb%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcabb8c2b-68b9-49bf-b35a-d948d2a61df7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4fd46328&sv=2)

Only one site can be ran per task group. To run multiple sites, you must make multiple task groups.

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/task-creation#monitor-setup)

Monitor Setup


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   The monitor section of a task group allows for easy mass-link-changing and allows users to get a better understanding of what their tasks are doing in real time.
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/task-creation#monitor-inputs)

Monitor Inputs

*   Monitor inputs are what PrismAIO uses when searching a website's sitemap to checkout a product. They are inputted under the "monitoring" section of the task group.
    

Info

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/task-creation#tab-info)

Keywords

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/task-creation#tab-keywords)

Direct Links

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/task-creation#tab-direct-links)

Variants

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/task-creation#tab-variants)

PID

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/task-creation#tab-pid)

There are four types of monitor inputs accepted by PrismAIO: keywords, direct links, variants, and PID.

Some sites can only accept a specific type of monitor input so be sure to follow the module guides on how to properly setup those sites.

*   If you are searching for the Yeezy 350 Zyon on a Shopify store, below is an example of a keyword group that you might run on a shopify store.
    
*   Place a (+) before every word that you want the bot to search for and place a (-) before every word that you want the bot to ignore.
    
    *   `(+yeezy,+350,+zyon,-pre,-toddler)`
        
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F213236379%2Fc25810b97810d1cd6893e321%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d8a5bc12&sv=2)

*   You can also use keyword groups to search for multiple different keyword sets independently such as the picture below. In this case, the bot will go for the Yeezy 350 Zyon OR the Yeezy 700 Waverunner - whichever product the bot picks up first is what it will go for.
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252F-MkNCarF99XonymaF_uX%252F-MkO2LtIlzIMNKMmwiFS%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D996bbb68-a5f3-4d35-af96-ab66207b9b1c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2023e85c&sv=2)

*   If you have an early link or would like to run a link for restocks, you can input the full item link into the monitor input. PrismAIO will automatically recognize the product URL and indicate above.
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F213236525%2F6a03166541edbae0e1fde810%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=51958b52&sv=2)

*   Variants are another monitor input used on sites like Shopify, Snipes USA, and Hibbett that match to a specific item and size.
    
*   Variants are usually provided by cook groups and used to run restock tasks.
    

**Enable Variants:**

*   To enable variants, navigate to `Task Group Settings` by clicking the three dots near the top-right section of the monitor section of the task group and click `Enable Variants`
    
*   You can input multiple variants on separate lines such as the picture below and just indicate the size on each task that you create within that group.
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F213240251%2F29f4cbb271f43616c7753d92%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9554a3a3&sv=2)

*   PID, short for product identification, is a monitor input that is tied to a specific product. It is most commonly used on footsites, Finish Line, JD Sports, and Yeezy Supply.
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/task-creation#task-group-monitoring)

Task Group Monitoring

Info

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/task-creation#tab-info-1)

Setup

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/task-creation#tab-setup)

FAQ

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/task-creation#tab-faq)

*   In PrismAIO, you will notice there is the option for two separate proxy groups and delays. In the monitoring section of the task group, that proxy list and delay box are used for **monitoring only.** Where as the proxy list and delay box displayed when creating a task are used for **adding to cart and checking out a product.**
    

*   The proxy list and delay in the monitor section are used for **monitoring only.** This means that the group itself is what will do the monitoring, **TASKS DO NOT DO INDIVIDUAL MONITORING.** For instance, if you see your bot on "Waiting for Product" that means that each individual task is waiting for the task group to find the product using the task group proxies. The only exception to this comes if your Shopify task becomes OOS while you are checking out, or if you are using variants. If this is the case, the bot will use the **TASK** proxies to monitor for that **SPECIFIC** size to come back in stock.
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252F-MkNCarF99XonymaF_uX%252F-MkO8e95yb5A05OYzasf%252Fmonitor.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D181ae4cd-2810-4d02-a5ff-ed89e266b7d8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=21cc9e91&sv=2)

What are "threads" A.K.A "monitor workers"?

*   Threads, in simpler terms, are like another monitoring task. The max threads the bot will use is 10. This is swiftly calculated by the bot to insure that your monitor proxies will not become banned. The bot takes into account a variety of factors, including how many proxies you have in the task group list, what your current task group delay is, and lastly what our "unbannable delay" is.
    

How much data do monitor "threads" use?

*   Monitor threads use roughly the same amount of data as a single task. With this though, the task group monitor is only looking for the product and in-stock sizes, and it does add-to-cart or checkout attempts which saves on data.
    

If my tasks have residential (resi) proxies as the TASK proxies and datacenter (DC/ISP) proxies as the MONITOR proxies, will they use data if the tasks are on "Waiting for Product"?

*   No, the tasks will not use the residential proxies to monitor for the product. If the tasks are on `Waiting for Product` or `Waiting for Restock`, they will use the DC proxies that are the monitor proxies to wait for the product to be live. The only case where the task will use the residential is if the site you are running is Shopify and the task proceeds to checkout but the product goes OOS. In that case, the task will CONTINUE to use the task proxies, in this case the residential ones.
    

How many monitor proxies do I need?

*   There is no set amount, but the more the better. If you run very low monitor delays, it is best to have many (25+) proxies.
    

Can I use no proxies (localhost) as the task group proxies?

*   You can, but it is not recommended to do it for more than 1 task group per site. So if you are running 5 task groups for Finish Line, don't run more that 1 task group without task group proxies.
    

Pro-tip: If you are running on a Shopify site with proxy protection and your datacenter proxies are throttled, run one task group on your localhost and your tasks with residential proxies. In this case, the bot should pickup the product faster rather than using residential proxies to monitor as they often are slower speeds.

Do the group proxies have to be the same as the task proxies?

*   No they do not. You can use two different groups for both - it does not matter if they are the same or not.
    

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/task-creation#task-creation)

Task Creation


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   After a task group has been created, tasks can be created by click the `+` icon at the top of the task group. Here, you can configure your tasks to what is needed to run the site. Depending on the site selected, different options will be available.
    

Profile

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/task-creation#tab-profile)

Delay

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/task-creation#tab-delay)

Proxy List

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/task-creation#tab-proxy-list)

Size

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/task-creation#tab-size)

Item Qty

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/task-creation#tab-item-qty)

Mode

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/task-creation#tab-mode)

Accounts

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/task-creation#tab-accounts)

Shipping Rate

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/task-creation#tab-shipping-rate)

*   Profile(s) used when creating the task.
    

*   Delay the task will retry on (retry list)
    

*   Proxy list used to checkout (checkout list)
    

*   Size(s) of the item you are going for.
    

*   Cart quantity
    

For almost all sites it is best to leave this at `1`

*   Used for Shopify only. Determines the mode the tasks will use to checkout. To learn about the differences between each mode, click here.
    

*   Rarely required but can be selected if desired. To learn about account creation, click [here](https://help2.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/settings#accounts)
    .
    

*   Never required but can be used to speed up checkout process on Shopify stores. To learn about shipping rates, click [here](https://help2.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/settings#shipping-rates)
    .
    

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/task-creation#editing-tasks)

Editing Tasks


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/task-creation#changing-monitor-inputs)

Changing Monitor Inputs

*   The monitor input can be easily changed by pasting the new monitor input over the old monitor input. Once pasted, the new monitor input will automatically save and tasks will begin to run for that.
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/task-creation#changing-task-data)

Changing Task Data

*   Tasks can be easily edited by holding `CTRL + A` to highlight all tasks or `CTRL + left click` to select certain tasks to edit. Once you have the desired tasks selected, click Update All or Update Sel. in the top-right corner of the task group to update.

# Domain Change | PrismAIO

*   Domain change releases often bring the most bot protection possible and involve changing to a completely new, often unknown site. To get started with a domain change release, create a task group for `Shopify Domain Change`
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/domain-change#task-creation)

Task Creation

*   Task creation for domain change is the exact same as setting up on a regular Shopify site. For domain change, you will always always want to use `Safe` mode.
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/domain-change#monitor-setup)

Monitor Setup

*   As soon as the product drops, you will want to add the **product URL** to the monitor input. It needs to be a direct product link if using the `Shopify Domain Change` site.
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252Fuploads%252FeZ1m4RO7iX8m1EUNpXxr%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc51b1139-2e3a-43f6-9cc5-2e420acdcdc8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d81a5d79&sv=2)

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/domain-change#browser-monitoring)

Browser Monitoring

*   For most domain change releases, you will want to have `Browser Monitoring` enabled. When enabled, a window will pop up where you have to manually add the product to cart once in order for the tasks to be able to add to cart.
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/domain-change#f.a.q)

F.A.Q

What mode do I run?

*   `Safe`
    

What should my delays be?

*   Monitor: `3500`
    
*   Task: `3500`
    

Do I use browser monitoring?

*   For most releases, have browser monitoring enabled.
    

What captcha should I use?

*   Have several `Shopify (Checkpoint)` harvesters open.
    

[PreviousSite Specific Setup](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup)
[NextFinish Line / JD Sports](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/finish-line-jd-sports)

# Finish Line / JD Sports | PrismAIO

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/finish-line-jd-sports#task-creation)

Task Creation


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Before creating tasks, you must create a new task group for Finish Line or JD Sports. For help on creating a new task group, follow [this guide.](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/task-creation)
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/finish-line-jd-sports#monitor-setup)

Monitor Setup

*   After creating a task group, you will want to use the product PID provided by our release guides or a third-party. Using a direct link **will not** work. The PID consists of the product id, product style, and color ID.
    
    *   `https://www.finishline.com/store/product/mens-nike-air-force-1-low-casual-shoes/prod795980?styleId=315122&colorId=111`
        
        *   The PID (monitor input) for this link would be `prod795980,315122,111`
            
        
    

When running for the same shoes on Finish Line and JD Sports, the monitor input will be the same for both sites.

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/finish-line-jd-sports#captcha-settings)

Captcha Settings

*   In order to cart a product on Finish Line or JD Sports when captcha is enabled, you must enable `Captcha` when creating tasks.
    
*   After that, open several default harvesters set to `JD Desktop` . Other third parties may work, but we recommend using default harvesters.
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/finish-line-jd-sports#task-creation-1)

Task Creation

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252F-MkTXEjrWsc8-g_zN3Qd%252F-MkTXL6B8vVNKXWiQ-Q4%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D310be5ae-6ded-4e9f-89b6-78a9db70e06b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=969c8982&sv=2)

Required Fields

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/finish-line-jd-sports#tab-required-fields)

Optional Fields

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/finish-line-jd-sports#tab-optional-fields)

*   **Profiles:** choose your profiles/profile group
    
*   **Captcha:** enable for almost all releases
    
*   **Delay:** task delay. Recommended to be left at `3000`
    
*   **Proxy List:** proxy list used to checkout (leave blank for localhost)
    
*   **Size:** size(s) the task will go for. If selecting multiple sizes, it will go for any size in your range
    

*   N/A
    

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/finish-line-jd-sports#faq)

FAQ


------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Will I need to "solve" captchas?

*   The answer is **no.** Finish Line uses V3 captchas so the only thing you need to make sure is that you are signed in to an email account with a 0.9 V3 rating. For more information on this rating, refer to your cook group.
    

How many harvesters do I need?

*   As many as you can have. There is no set ratio or recommended amount.
    

Do I need proxies in my harvesters?

*   If using more than 1 harvester, you must have proxies in the harvester.

# Hibbett Restock Guide | PrismAIO

*   Before setting up for Hibbett restocks, please familiarize your self with general task creation which can be found [here](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/hibbett)
    .
    

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/hibbett/hibbett-restock-guide#setting-up-for-hibbett-restocks)

**Setting Up For Hibbett Restocks:**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   The fastest and most efficient way to run for Hibbett restocks is by using **SKU** and **cloud** **mode**. Variants will be provided via share links for certain shoes in the Discord channel titled "run-for-restocks" which will be updated periodically.
    
*   Hibbett restocks occur in 30 minute intervals. Knowing the exact time they will restock is not possible so it is best to check monitors to see at what interval the product you are trying to go for is restocking.
    
*   In order to run restocks with variants, it is **highly recommended to use the "Cloud" feature** to maximize the product you can run. You will want to start tasks 5-7 minutes before the expected restock as payment tokens expire and thus do not allow tasks to be ran 24/7.
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252Fuploads%252FVDg6xzDKI7EXzNDrbksj%252FScreenshot%25202023-03-13%2520at%25207.42.42%2520AM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D44d852f9-cfae-48d7-8c57-8ae412d64cc1&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a0ad5098&sv=2)

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/hibbett/hibbett-restock-guide#cloud-monitoring)

Cloud Monitoring


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   If cloud mode I selected, tasks will utilize cloud monitoring. Instead of showing a timer, tasks will say "Waiting for Restock" and are waiting for the cloud monitor to ping and tell tasks to spam payment.
    

Note: tasks must be started before the cloud ping goes off.

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/hibbett/hibbett-restock-guide#faq)

FAQ

Why am I getting retrying payment?

*   Retrying payment means that the product is out of stock and that the task is trying to submit the payment again in hopes that the product comes back in stock.
    

Should I use residential or datacenter proxies?

*   Residential proxies are required.
    

What delays should I run for restocks?

*   Speed plays a big factor in Hibbett restocks. For best chances on restocks, it is best to drop task delay to about 1000 right before the restock. Monitor delay does not matter if you are running **with drop time.** Note: DO NOT run 24/7, only run it for a short period of time during a potential restock.
    

How long should I let my tasks run before stopping?

*   It is recommended to stop tasks about 1 minute after the potential restock.
    

Do I need to use the "Restock" mode?

*   Restock mode is slightly faster than cloud mode, but the restock mode usually reamins locked. It is best to use cloud mode unless otherwise made note in Discord.
    

[PreviousHibbett](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/hibbett)
[NextOffspring / Office](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/offspring-office)

Last updated 2 years ago

Was this helpful?
