# Quick Task API | PrismAIO

The Quick Task API format is as follows:

Copy

    https://dashboard.prismaio.com?url=URL

[](https://help.prismaio.com/misc.-guides/quick-task-api#url-instructions)

**URL Instructions**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/misc.-guides/quick-task-api#product-link-format)

Product Link Format

For the product link format, a link can either be just the product or the product with a desired variant. For example, if one wanted to make a quick task for this [product](https://kith.com/collections/footwear/products/new-balance-made-in-us-990v4-elderberry-pigment)
, the desired format for a quick task link would be:

Copy

    https://dashboard.prismaio.com?url=https://kith.com/collections/footwear/products/new-balance-made-in-us-990v4-elderberry-pigment

If you want to specify the variant for a product, the following is also a valid quick task link which will _override_ the user’s default size:

Copy

    https://dashboard.prismaio.com?url=https://kith.com/collections/footwear/products/new-balance-made-in-us-990v4-elderberry-pigment?variant=16319713804357
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/misc.-guides/quick-task-api#add-to-cart-format)

Add to Cart Format

PrismAIO allows a user to input an add-to-cart link as the url. For example, this is also a valid quick task link:

Copy

    https://dashboard.prismaio.com?url=https://kith.com/cart/16319713804357:1

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/misc.-guides/quick-task-api#mass-link-change)

Mass Link Change

PrismAIO allows a user to mass link change an existing task group to a new product. The URL to mass link change is below where `PRODUCT_URL` is changed to the product URL of what the user is trying to change to:

Copy

    https://dashboard.prismaio.com/?url=PRODUCT_URL&action=update

[PreviousHow to Access Crash Logs](https://help.prismaio.com/misc.-guides/how-to-access-crash-logs)

# Captcha | PrismAIO

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/captcha#create-and-manage-captcha-harvesters)

Create and Manage Captcha Harvesters


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Captcha harvesters can be accessed via the "Harvesters" section which is located in the setting page of the bot or by clicking "Captcha" in the top right-hand section of the bot.
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252F-Mk5PaGXdVFradIl3sJW%252F-Mk5Pzhb8ea0N8Ckd6YP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dded59af8-37c9-4a22-ac73-73b5bcb18c81&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5e5cc4c4&sv=2)

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/captcha#creation)

Creation

*   Once in the "Harvesters" tab, you can create new harvesters by clicking on the "Create" button which is located near the top right-hand corner of the bot.
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/captcha#logging-in)

Logging In

*   Log in by clicking the middle button (Google icon)
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252F-Mk5PaGXdVFradIl3sJW%252F-Mk5QrKenLylYm17rboN%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D869f1365-813d-4c5c-832c-442cfdb5f23f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=77031648&sv=2)

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/captcha#change-captcha-settings-in-task-groups)

Change Captcha Settings in Task Groups

*   With the addition of third-party harvesters, you must change your task group captcha settings in order to use them. This can be done by fully opening the task group and looking on the left-hand side. There is a file called "Captcha Settings." Click on it to expand it.

Third Party Captcha Solutions


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Start Here

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/captcha#tab-start-here)

2Captcha

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/captcha#tab-id-2captcha-1)

Use the other columns for help on setting up third party captcha solutions. To the right of this tab, you will notice four different tabs corresponding to a different captcha solution. While they are very similar in nature, it's best to have API keys for each third party to ensure you are covered on drop day.

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/captcha#id-2captcha-setup-guide)

**2Captcha Setup Guide**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Create an Account:

*   The first thing you will need to do is create an account for 2Captcha which can be created [here](https://2captcha.com/auth/register)
    .
    

Adding Funds:

*   Upon creating an account, you will need to add funds to 2Captcha. This captcha service is **NOT** free.
    
*   You can add funds by clicking the "Add Funds" button on their dashboard.
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F261311629%2F873c5faac94d3f310202df83%2F2cap.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=89577f2f&sv=2)

Getting your API Key:

*   After adding funds to your account, you will need to copy your API key to add it to the bot.
    
*   DO NOT share this API key with anyone.
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F261314577%2Fa46aad0aaf61b533a8269a29%2F2cap%2Bapi.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a73d7ce2&sv=2)

    .

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F261327686%2F3f1b687b86cc99ee4c0c66d8%2Fapi%2Bpage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=73dc8512&sv=2)

**How to Add an API Key:**

*   An API key can be added by clicking the top right "Create" button.
    
*   You will then need to choose you harvester type (Anti Captcha or 2Captcha).
    
*   After selecting the provider, paste your API key into the API key tab and click the save button.

Once you have selected the one you want, any captcha requests for that task group will be sent to the selected source.

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/captcha#autosolve-by-aycd-setup)

AutoSolve by AYCD Setup


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

AutoSolve by AYCD is a product that aids in solving captchas. For more information on it, refer to their site which can be found [here](https://aycd.io/)
.

AYCD Toolbox + AutoSolve are **NOT FREE** products and both require subscriptions. To purchase, head over to their site.

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/captcha#setting-up-autosolve)

**Setting Up AutoSolve:**

BEFORE proceeding, please review ALL the guides provided by AYCD.

[https://aycd.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/sections/360007407234-AutoSolve?page=1#articles](https://aycd.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/sections/360007407234-AutoSolve?page=1#articles)

*   After successfully purchasing both Toolbox and AutoSolve, head on over to AYCD to login and than go to the [AutoSolve Dashboard](https://dash.autosolve.aycd.io/)
    .
    
*   On the dashboard, you will see two important boxes: one that has your "Access Token" and another that has the "AutoSolve Bot API Keys"
    

**Access Token:**

*   The access token is required to run AutoSolve. To copy the access token, simply click the box that says "Copy Access Token"
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F265484561%2F617a39ad7b89f67db845d30b%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a180994b&sv=2)

**AutoSolve Bot API Keys:**

*   Next you will want to create an AuotSolve API key for Prism. To do this, click the create button and name the API key. Next, find the newly created key in the drop down menu and click the copy button.
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F265484918%2F0a2cab85c2f28501d1e75e8a%2Ftempsnip.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ebe7674c&sv=2)

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/captcha#adding-access-token-api-key-to-prism)

**Adding Access Token + API Key to Prism:**

*   AutoSolve setup can be accessed via the harvesters section in the settings tab of the bot. In order to add your AutoSolve keys, you first must create a new harvester in the top right. Upon creating a new harvester, you must change the type to "AutoSolve"
    
*   After you have done that, you will paste your API key and access token above into their corresponding boxes.
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F265657707%2Fc7e0deb507c87391f9ebed90%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=101e97c5&sv=2)

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/captcha#h_8fa0201d9e)

**Setting-up Autosolve for Footsites (third party captcha services):**

1) Check the connections tab in Autosolve and make sure that your prism is showing up here. If you do not see Prism listed below, go to the `Troubleshooting` section of the guide below.

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F391087655%2Fc57e9da378a0fe156027f5e9%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=65fd2a39&sv=2)

2) To use third-party captcha services, go back to the Autosolve tab. Your third-party captcha services should all show up under services. If you do not see them, you will need to go back to the AYCD dashboard and enter each third-party API key on the AYCD website.

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F391091183%2Fa581934398a35cff65f9b0eb%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ff52269c&sv=2)

3) Make sure there is a checkmark next to each third-party service you would like to use and set the priority on the left-hand side by dragging them around.

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F391103532%2Fa7824b4901b18c7b2b1d5f18%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a2eb10ba&sv=2)

4) Press the green `Connect` button on the top left corner.

5) Now go to prism and in your task group, make sure your captcha source is set to `Auto Solve`. After this step, you are all set and ready to run tasks with auto solve for Footsites!

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/captcha#h_be792a487f)

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F391104870%2Fa4ab40aede9ef945fefa2ac2%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=56c0394f&sv=2)

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/captcha#h_adf63c3587)

**Setting-up Autosolve for YeezySupply:**

1) Check the connections tab in Autosolve and make sure that your prism is showing up here. If you do not see Prism listed below, go to the `Troubleshooting` section of the guide below.

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F391087655%2Fc57e9da378a0fe156027f5e9%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=65fd2a39&sv=2)

2) Once you have confirmed that auto solve is connected and showing up in AYCD, start auto solve on the actual emails that you plan on using for this drop by clicking on the `Accounts` tab.

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F391094004%2Fe7891e0ad287adc64792c1ed%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=758e1001&sv=2)

3) Make sure that only `OneClick` is showing up connected.

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F391104548%2Ff3cbaa5a5665c2e15636e8b9%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5a64dd61&sv=2)

4) Now go to prism and in your task group, make sure your captcha source is set to `Auto Solve`. After this step, you are all set and ready to run tasks with auto solve for Yeezysupply.

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F391095073%2Fd24ed38c0a7f9d74a1f68932%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=43b34377&sv=2)

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/captcha#h_502e054eef)

**Troubleshooting:**

**If you do not see your Prism connected to AYCD, try these steps:**

1) Restart both PrismAIO and AYCD and try again.

2) If it still does not show up, go to your Prism and delete the AYCD harvester.

3) Then go to AYCD's dashboard website and delete your existing Prism API key.

4) Generate a new API key. Then back to Prism and create a new Autosolve harvester. Enter your information and check again.

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/captcha#faq)

FAQ


------------------------------------------------------------------------

Do I need to use proxies?

*   Yes. If you are using more than one harvester, you must use proxies. Note: Shopify harvesters DO NOT need proxies.
    

Does each harvester need to have a different email?

*   Yes. If you are using more than one harvester, you need to make sure each harvester is logged into a different account.
    

What is the difference between "Shopify Checkout" and "Shopify Checkpoint"?

*   "Shopify Checkout" will only show a captcha if it is a checkout captcha.
    
*   "Shopify Checkpoint" will only show a captcha if it is a checkpoint captcha.
    
*   In order to successfully checkout on Shopify sites with anti-bot, you need to have **at least 1 of each harvester open.**
    

Do I need to login to my harvester every time I open the bot?

*   No. Once you are logged into the harvester, your account will not be logged out.
    

Can I select multiple captcha sources per task group?

*   No. Each task group can only have one captcha source.
    

Which harvester types should I use?

*   Below is a table displaying what harvester types is recommended.
    

Footsites

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/captcha#tab-footsites)

Shopify

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/captcha#tab-shopify)

Yeezy Supply

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/captcha#tab-yeezy-supply)

Snipes USA

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/captcha#tab-snipes-usa)

Offspring / Office

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/captcha#tab-offspring-office)

Foot Locker EU

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/captcha#tab-foot-locker-eu)

Supreme

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/captcha#tab-supreme)

Use **any** third party solution (2Captcha, Anti-Captcha, CapMonster, and/or AutoSolve) all work the fine/ the same.

Only use **default** harvesters for intitial, third party can be used but will be slower.

Only use **default or AutoSolve** harvesters

Use **any** third party solution (2Captcha, Anti-Captcha, CapMonster, and/or AutoSolve) all work the fine/ the same.

Use **any** third party solution (2Captcha, Anti-Captcha, CapMonster, and/or AutoSolve) all work the fine/ the same.

Use **any** third party solution (2Captcha, Anti-Captcha, CapMonster, and/or AutoSolve) all work the fine/ the same.

Only use **default** harvesters or AYCD AutoSolve with AI

[PreviousSettings](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/settings)
[NextAutomations](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/automations)

# Pacsun | PrismAIO

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/pacsun#task-creation)

Task Creation


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Before creating tasks, you must create a new task group for Pacsun. For help on creating a new task group, follow [this guide.](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/task-creation)
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/pacsun#monitor-setup)

Monitor Setup

*   After creating a task group, you will want to use the product PID provided by our release guides or a third-party. Using a direct link **will not** work. The PID can be found in the product URL link.
    
    *   `https://www.pacsun.com/space-jam-tune-squad-t-shirt-0097438400007.html`
        
        *   The PID (monitor input) for this link would be `0097438400007`
            
        
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/pacsun#task-creation-1)

Task Creation

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252Fuploads%252Fo5Nf7M7myybI4tY7NXst%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da8288aac-2fa1-4b9f-8bac-4f93cac03120&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=41557b59&sv=2)

Required Fields

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/pacsun#tab-required-fields)

Optional Fields

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/pacsun#tab-optional-fields)

*   **Profiles:** choose your profiles/profile group
    
*   **Delay:** task delay. Recommended to be left at `3500`
    
*   **Proxy List:** proxy list used to checkout (leave blank for localhost)
    
*   **Size:** size(s) the task will go for. If selecting multiple sizes, it will go for any size in your range
    

*   N/A

[NextSSENSE](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/ssense)

# Yeezy Supply | PrismAIO

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/yeezy-supply#task-creation)

Task Creation


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Before creating tasks, you must create a new task group for `Yeezy Supply`. For help on creating a new task group, follow [this guide.](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/task-creation)
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/yeezy-supply#monitor-setup)

Monitor Setup

*   After creating a task group, you will want to use the SKU of the product provided by our release guides or can be found at the end or the URL. Using a URL **will not** work.
    
    *   `https://www.yeezysupply.com/product/GX5049`
        
        *   The monitor input would be: `GX5049`
            
        
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/yeezy-supply#captcha-settings)

Captcha Settings

*   In order to pass the Yeezy Supply splash, you must have several Google accounts with a V2 one-click status.
    
*   You can check the score of your Gmail by logging into your Google account and going to [this site](https://recaptcha-demo.appspot.com/recaptcha-v3-request-scores.php)
    .
    
*   There will be no "captcha" for you to solve. For those unaware, V3 captcha means that there is nothing to solve as it is based on the V3 score. Just have your harvesters open and leave them be.
    

300:1 task:Gmail ratio

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/yeezy-supply#task-creation-1)

Task Creation

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252F-MkTRP2zCstpXOpdbNU_%252F-MkTT7XyceozHzSQ6a7V%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8fa2cd75-2d7b-4750-b847-0d179eb87f92&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2f19ce24&sv=2)

Required Fields

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/yeezy-supply#tab-required-fields)

Optional Fields

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/yeezy-supply#tab-optional-fields)

*   **Profiles:** choose your profiles/profile group
    
*   **Delay:** task delay. Recommended to be left at `3000`
    
*   **Proxy List:** proxy list used to checkout (leave blank for localhost)
    
*   **Size:** size(s) the task will go for. If selecting multiple sizes, it will go for any size in your range
    

*   N/A
    

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/yeezy-supply#faq)

FAQ


---------------------------------------------------------------------

How many captcha harvesters do I need to have open?

*   One harvester for every 300 to 500 tasks. You can run more tasks per harvester, but the more harvesters the better.
    

What should my monitor delay be?

*   `3000`
    

Should I use residential or DC/ISP proxies?

*   A mix is recommended but both have yielded great results.
    

When should I start my tasks?

*   You should start your tasks anytime when queue is up. Tasks will automatically wait until the sale is live to start using data and captchas.
    

How can I open task browser?

*   Once a task carts, you can open the task browser by right clicking the task and clicking `Open Browser`
    

Why can't I pass splash?

*   The main reason is due to your Gmails having too low of a V3 score.
    

Does 2Captcha/Anti-Captcha/Cap Monster/AutoSolve work?

*   They do but we HIGHLY recommend you do not use them.
    

Why am I getting `Max Cookie Attempts`?

*   This means your proxy + bot were unable to generate an Akamai cookie needed to cart. Try using new task proxies next time.
    

Should I use default harvesters or AYCD AutoSolve?

*   They both have the exact same pass rate/success.
    

Do I use `Yeezy Supply Queue` or `Yeezy Supply Code` harvesters?

*   Always use queue harvesters. If a code harvester is needed, one will open for you.
    

[PreviousFNL/JD Automation SKU List](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/finish-line-jd-sports/fnl-jd-automation-sku-list)
[NextHibbett](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/hibbett)

Last updated 3 years ago

# How to Access Crash Logs | PrismAIO

[](https://help.prismaio.com/misc.-guides/how-to-access-crash-logs#h_09ca71d1cc)

**Windows:**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Path File: `AppData/Roaming/PrismAIO/crash.log`
    

Step 1:

*   Go to your desktop and click CTRL + R on your keyboard to open the run window. Type into the box: `%appdata%` and press OK.
    

[![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F288565739%2Fb1bdd3a1589775f78fcf5375%2Fimage.png%3Fexpires%3D1618610400%26signature%3D823818f0b9f0a0fe60a91c4c82d25bd63e31a5d71cd0ffa146178b1d51d21e30&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d16ae8f5&sv=2)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/288565739/b1bdd3a1589775f78fcf5375/image.png?expires=1618610400&signature=823818f0b9f0a0fe60a91c4c82d25bd63e31a5d71cd0ffa146178b1d51d21e30)

Step 2:

*   Scroll down and locate the PrismAIO folder. Double click it to open it.
    

[![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F288565828%2Fd59cd94fe9d41d38eddc77c4%2Fimage.png%3Fexpires%3D1618610400%26signature%3D5ffb3309f16ff14cd95e4835815e84e39dd0e2d9070c1c2a6538031c60ef2116&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=102683bd&sv=2)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/288565828/d59cd94fe9d41d38eddc77c4/image.png?expires=1618610400&signature=5ffb3309f16ff14cd95e4835815e84e39dd0e2d9070c1c2a6538031c60ef2116)

Step 3:

*   Find the file called "crash" and drag it directly into your Discord ticket. If the file is too big, open the file first using notepad. There should be a timestamp showing "engine exited with code 2" and a recent timestamp and error code above it towards the bottom of the file. Please copy and paste that into the ticket.
    

[![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F288565995%2Fc4f28f10d72b1218ef336ceb%2Fimage.png%3Fexpires%3D1618610400%26signature%3D16c8ed3eb5fc2b4e8617eca13b0bc6116eabbe5651bd879dcb8f8b590ffbb421&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6b09a34a&sv=2)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/288565995/c4f28f10d72b1218ef336ceb/image.png?expires=1618610400&signature=16c8ed3eb5fc2b4e8617eca13b0bc6116eabbe5651bd879dcb8f8b590ffbb421)

[](https://help.prismaio.com/misc.-guides/how-to-access-crash-logs#h_c86898291e)

**Mac:**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Path File: `/Library/Application Support/PrismAIO/crash.log`
    

Step 1:

*   Navigate to finder and once you are in finder, move your coursor all the way to the top of your computer and find `"Go"` and click on it.
    

[![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F288566225%2Ff7c39b623050b3d5706d3bcb%2Fimage.png%3Fexpires%3D1618610400%26signature%3Df2d27689fc7c927cb4bc2400cf3e5afafd042bae9838eed1bf3cd712b9288dce&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c65e7cf&sv=2)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/288566225/f7c39b623050b3d5706d3bcb/image.png?expires=1618610400&signature=f2d27689fc7c927cb4bc2400cf3e5afafd042bae9838eed1bf3cd712b9288dce)

Step 2:

*   While in the go menu, hold the `"Option"` key to reveal a folder called `"Library"`
    

[![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F288566281%2F0832e65b9130b02c189eafff%2Fimage.png%3Fexpires%3D1618610400%26signature%3Dc64d7bd51e346ed4fff73c5f380fc3f10648d0e81bda25c3a532adc82a92b323&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c0394ebe&sv=2)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/288566281/0832e65b9130b02c189eafff/image.png?expires=1618610400&signature=c64d7bd51e346ed4fff73c5f380fc3f10648d0e81bda25c3a532adc82a92b323)

Step 3:

*   Navigate to the `"Application Support"` and than to `"PrismAIO"`
    

[![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F288566347%2F6cdfa797c60eff653289b337%2Fimage.png%3Fexpires%3D1618610400%26signature%3D3a7d16caa226bc9b7680aa7ed023c57ff1eeb19d0bc2e4d9e6613575cc465207&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fb8dfd57&sv=2)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/288566347/6cdfa797c60eff653289b337/image.png?expires=1618610400&signature=3a7d16caa226bc9b7680aa7ed023c57ff1eeb19d0bc2e4d9e6613575cc465207)

Step 4:

*   Double click `"PrismAIO"` to open it and find the file called `"Crash"` Once you do, drag that file directly into your Discord ticket. If the file is too big, open the file first using text edit. There should be a timestamp showing "engine exited with code 2" and a recent timestamp and error code above it towards the bottom of the file. Please copy and paste that into the ticket.

# SSENSE | PrismAIO

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/ssense#task-creation)

Task Creation


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Before creating tasks, you must create a new task group for SSENSE. For help on creating a new task group, follow [this guide.](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/task-creation)
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/ssense#monitor-setup)

Monitor Setup

*   After creating a task group, you will want to use the product PID provided by our release guides or a third-party. Using a direct link **will not** work. The PID can be found in the product URL link.
    
    *   `https://www.ssense.com/en-us/men/product/ambush/off-white-rubber-chelsea-boots/7616491`
        
        *   The PID (monitor input) for this link would be `7616491`
            
        
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/ssense#task-creation-1)

Task Creation

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252Fuploads%252FWEATb31TNic6VTw12z30%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc822b91d-aa7a-428e-8e4c-77142c203206&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=60de3416&sv=2)

Required Fields

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/ssense#tab-required-fields)

Optional Fields

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/ssense#tab-optional-fields)

*   **Profiles:** choose your profiles/profile group
    
*   **Payment Method:** select `card` to use the card on the profile or `Alipay` to have an Alipay webhook sent to your success webhook.
    
*   **Accounts:** Some product need accounts. Select the account(s) you want to use.
    
*   **Delay:** task delay. Recommended to be left at `3500`
    
*   **Proxy List:** proxy list used to checkout (leave blank for localhost)
    
*   **Size:** size(s) the task will go for. If selecting multiple sizes, it will go for any size in your range
    

*   N/A

# Footsites (North America) | PrismAIO

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/footsites-north-america#task-creation)

Task Creation


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Before creating tasks, you must create a new task group for the footsite you want to run on. For help on creating a new task group, follow [this guide.](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/task-creation)
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/footsites-north-america#monitor-setup)

Monitor Setup

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252F-MkT5DmDkPkYOLf6Toos%252F-MkTMLX1Fn9YQNyTM8OV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3465479b-e322-4693-861a-2aa3d4e0090f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fe678098&sv=2)

*   **Product ID:** use the product PID provided by our release guides or a third-party. Using a direct link will not work.
    
*   **Proxy List:** used for monitoring only. Can be the same as your task list.
    
*   **Delay:** monitor delay. Recommended to be left at `5000`
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/footsites-north-america#captcha-settings)

Captcha Settings

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fgblobscdn.gitbook.com%2Fassets%252F-MjlAl2GRDRXdOEoyrEH%252F-MjlCYaGF9SPBGA41I6I%252F-MjlGI4PP5MEHCGa8AAb%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9264e824-3423-4385-85de-6ed91532b4db&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3b0f6644&sv=2)

*   Captcha setting that will be used to solve any Queue-It captchas. Recommended to use **any third party solution.** For help on third party setup, follow [this guide.](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/captcha#third-party-captcha-solutions)
    

Captchas are required for **Queue-It only!** DataDome captchas are solved by Prism.

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/footsites-north-america#task-creation-1)

Task Creation

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252F-MkT5DmDkPkYOLf6Toos%252F-MkTMoWwr9zcNh2B0mgR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc27c3b7a-c40c-423e-bee8-3802ac866938&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d9663ff2&sv=2)

Required Fields

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/footsites-north-america#tab-required-fields)

Optional Fields

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/footsites-north-america#tab-optional-fields)

*   **Profiles:** choose your profiles/profile group
    
*   **Delay:** task delay. Recommended to be left at `5000`
    
*   **Proxy List:** proxy list used to checkout (leave blank for localhost)
    
*   **Size:** size(s) the task will go for. If selecting multiple sizes, it will go for any size in your range.
    

*   **Account List:** FLX accounts the tasks will use
    
*   **Gift Card List:** Gift card list the tasks will use
    

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/footsites-north-america#queue-it)

Queue-It


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   There is a common misconception that if the release uses Queue-It then Geetest will not be used and this is **wrong**. Regardless of the queue type, DataDome with Geetest will always be in use.
    
    *   For those unfamiliar with Queue-It, it is another queue type that Footsites use. Queue-It requries a recaptcha V2 (standard captcha) to enter the queue.
        
    *   DataDome is the anti-bot that Footsites use and when your proxy becomes blocked, a captcha will be needed. Prism will solve all GeeTest captcha **automatically**.
        
    

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/footsites-north-america#status-codes)

Status Codes


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Info

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/footsites-north-america#tab-info)

Status Codes

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/footsites-north-america#tab-status-codes-1)

*   Some errors are simply unpredictable so they don't have a designated status in the bot. If you encounter one of those errors, you can search the error here to see what it means.
    

Waiting for Product:

*   The task is waiting for the monitor to pickup the product. If you are stuck here but the drop is live, change your monitor proxies.
    

Waiting xxhr xxm xxs:

*   This means that the task is waiting for the countdown on the site to end.
    

Queue:

*   For most footsites drops, they will put up a queue and slowly let tasks/users through. This status is perfectly normal and you must let the bot run.
    

Queue (Perma):

*   During high-traffic periods, footsites will put up a permeant (perma) queue. This status means that they are not allowing anyone to pass the queue and access the product page.
    
*   Can also occur due to region locked releases. For example, US proxies will not work on some CA releases.
    

Out of Stock, retrying...:

*   This is the most important status and is what you want most of your tasks to be at. Footsites release stock over time, and not at once, so this status means that the task is continuing to try and add the product to cart until they add more stock.
    

Generating Session:

*   One of the first statuses you will see will be generating session. Each task must generate a session. If you find your tasks stuck on this status, you must change your proxies.
    

Solving Datadome:

*   Your tasks are waiting for you to solve the Datadome captcha. If you are stuck there, stop using third party solvers and solve the captcha.
    

IP Banned:

*   IP Banned means that the proxy or IP address you are using in the bot is banned and cannot access the product page. For the most part, the only way to fix this status is to change proxies.
    

Rate Limited:

*   Rate limit occurs when you are sending too many requests from a single IP address. Some proxies are rate limited by default so make sure to test your proxies before the drop.
    

Cart Expired:

*   This usually happens when one of your tasks has carted and another task using the same billing profile attempts to cart again. Both carts will be cleared and you will get this status. The only way to combat this is to run more unique billing profiles for your tasks.
    

Proxy Error:

*   Proxy error means bad proxy. Change your proxy list.
    

Request Timed Out:

*   This error means that the task could not establish a connection to the site. Causes for this include slow proxies and a site that is under a lot of traffic.
    

Error Adding to Cart:

*   Sometimes a size will give an error when you try to add to cart via the bot or even manually. If you see this error, just let it run.
    

Unknown Response \[400\]:

*   Usually means a bad prrofile if it occurs before a billing step
    
*   Can also be bot related.
    

Unknown Response \[403\]:

*   Another way to say rate limited. Change proxies if you encounter this.
    

Unknown Response \[404\]:

*   Means that the site or page is not found OR the bot is not working.
    

Unknown Response \[418\]:

*   This is normal as the site is experiencing heavy traffic. Just let your tasks run.
    

Unknown Response \[421\]:

*   This is normal as the site is experiencing heavy traffic. Just let your tasks run.
    

Unknown Response \[502\]:

*   Site error
    

Unknown Response \[503\]:

*   Site error
    

Task Crashed:

*   Rarely occurs but can happen. Open a ticket if you get this error.
    

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/footsites-north-america#faq)

FAQ


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/footsites-north-america#general-faq)

General FAQ

What is Adyen?

*   Adyen is footsite's payment processor. They are very strict on checkout information so during footsite drops you might receive a lot of cancellation emails. This is not the bot's fault, but solely based off the information that was used to checkout.
    

Can I use the same profile multiple times?

*   You can, but it is not recommended.
    

What type of proxies are recommended?

*   For initial drops, a mix of residential and datacenter proxies are recommended.
    

What are cart holds?

*   Footsites use a cart hold system to try and make a release fair. When you add a product to cart during release time, theoretically the product will be held in your cart for around 10 minutes to give you time to checkout. With this, the product may show as out of stock very fast. Most of the time, this does not mean that it is actually out of stock! During footsite drops, people who were not successful in checking out will have their cart lost. This typically happens in waves of about 5 to 10 minutes. When these waves occur, you will see a heavy influx in checkouts.
    

Why am I getting payment declined?

*   Sometimes payment failures/declines are a result of your bank declining the transaction. But with the recent changes to footsites, your task will show payment declined if you have already checked out that product on one site using the same profile. With this, it is highly recommended to use as many profiles as possible.
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/footsites-north-america#proxies)

Proxies

If I use Residential proxies as my TASK proxies, will they use data while monitoring?

*   They will **not** as long as they are on "Waiting for Product" or "Waiting for Restock." But as soon as the product is picked up it will begin to use the proxies that are assigned to your tasks.
    

Why am I seeing "IP Banned"?

*   IP banned occurs when the bot continues to try and add a product to the cart but the product page has been pulled. It is just a page ban that can be resolved by restarting tasks.
    

Why am I seeing "Rate Limit"?

*   Rate limit occurs when you send too many requests from a single IP in a short amount of time. This can occur if you are running low delays or not enough proxies. The only way to fix this is too use a new set of proxies.
    
*   With this though, some footsite products are rate limited for everyone. If you try and add to cart manually and get an error, the bot showing "rate limit" is a reflection of that.
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/footsites-north-america#accounts)

**Accounts**

Can I use the same FLX accounts for multiple tasks?

*   **No**! Each task must be assigned one account as using the same account multiple times will cause lots of errors.
    

[PreviousAutomations](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/automations)
[NextFootsites (USA) Automation SKU List](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/footsites-north-america/automation-sku-list)

# Offspring / Office | PrismAIO

*   Offspring is a site that often conducts raffles for their hyped shoes, but on occasion, will drop pairs on the site. When they do drop, it is typically at a completely random time. Office is their sister site, exactly the same in terms of flow.
    

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/offspring-office#task-creation)

Task Creation


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Before creating tasks, you must create a new task group for `Offspring` of `Office`. For help on creating a new task group, follow [this guide.](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/task-creation)
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/offspring-office#monitor-setup)

Monitor Setup

*   After creating a task group, you will want to use the product PID provided by our release guides or a third-party to the monitor input. The PID consists of the product PID in the title of the product.
    
    *   `https://www.offspring.co.uk/view/product/offspring_catalog/5,21/2021996289`
        
    *   `https://www.office.co.uk/view/product/office_catalog/5,21/2021996289`
        
        *   For these links, the PID would be `2021996289`
            
        
    

Using a direct URL link **will not work.**

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/offspring-office#webhook-setup)

Webhook Setup

*   Webhooks are required to recieve PayPal checkout links. For help on setting up webhooks, refer to [this guide.](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/settings#general)
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/offspring-office#paypal-setup)

PayPal Setup

*   PayPal can be manually enabled by toggling the `Use PayPal` toggle or in the event your credit card fails to checkout, it will result to sending a PayPal checkout link.
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/offspring-office#captcha-settings)

Captcha Settings

*   Offspring and Office both require a captcha token for each add to cart request so make sure you have `Offspring` captcha harvesters open (even if you are running Office) or a 3rd party provider set in task group captcha settings (recommended).
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/offspring-office#task-creation-1)

Task Creation

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252F-MkTe2EtgGSrsErTKDNW%252F-MkTeuXaM1SHAiOGYo0P%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8e5e64da-d929-4ca8-b74d-56f921f4ff1c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=48de8315&sv=2)

Required Fields

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/offspring-office#tab-required-fields)

Optional Fields

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/offspring-office#tab-optional-fields)

*   **Profiles:** choose your profiles/profile group
    
*   **Use PayPal:** for most tasks have this enabled
    
*   **Delay:** task delay. Recommended to be left at `4000` and drop the delay at drop time
    
*   **Proxy List:** proxy list used to checkout (leave blank for localhost)
    
*   **Size:** size(s) the task will go for. If selecting multiple sizes, it will go for any size in your range
    

*   N/A
    

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/offspring-office#faq)

FAQ


-------------------------------------------------------------------------

Do Offspring / Office ship worldwide?

*   They ship to many countries, including the United States, but often shipping is very expensive ($55ish to the United States). But please check with a test task or manually to confirm that they ship to your location.
    

What time do they drop?

*   Drops are almost random (shock drop). Sometimes they are early in the morning or even late at night. Stay connected to the Offspring monitor provided in the Discord or refer to your cook group's monitor instead.
    

What sizes do they drop?

*   Both sites typically drop in UK sizes so make sure you are going for the proper US size that you want.
    

Can I use the same proxies at the same time if I am running both Offspring and Office?

*   We do not recommend doing this from our own testing. If you are running both sites at the same time, please use different proxies.

# Settings | PrismAIO

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/settings#general)

General


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/settings#webhooks)

Webhooks

*   Paste your webbook into the corresponding section and click save. To test the webbook, click test.
    

Info

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/settings#tab-info)

Discord Webhook Setup

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/settings#tab-discord-webhook-setup)

Slack Webhook Setup

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/settings#tab-slack-webhook-setup)

Paste your webhook into the corresponding section and click save. To test the webbook, click test.

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252F-MkICNVZR9nJYoAl4CY_%252F-MkIDcDCY9Vtoj4VstXa%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7b30cbff-784f-4f46-8626-923c1f41418d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9d0afeeb&sv=2)

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/settings#creating-a-webhook)

**Creating a Webhook**

*   A Discord webhook is used to not only see PrismAIO success, but also **required** to receive PayPal checkout links.
    

Step 1:

*   Create your own Discord server by clicking the "+ - Add A Server" Icon on Discord.
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F206531241%2F04886ea7ee1f0e6f60045a3f%2Fdiscord%2Bcreate%2Bserver.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7fd9fc65&sv=2)

Step 2:

*   Click on the `create a server` button and fill out the necessary information to create your server.
    
*   Once your server is all setup, you will than want to head to `server settings` tab.
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F206533992%2F295d49fe0c5005faa4bc773f%2FAnnotation%2B2020-05-05%2B163551.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=36e98e44&sv=2)

*   In server settings, head over to the `webhooks`tab.
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F206534277%2F6ed726b13a3d14d8540c025b%2FAnnotation%2B2020-05-05%2B163911.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cb8ad75a&sv=2)

*   Click on the `Create Webhook` button to create your webhook. Choose what channel you want the webhook to go too. **Make sure to copy that link as it is needed for the bot.**
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/settings#creating-a-webhook-1)

**Creating a Webhook**

*   A Slack webhook is used to not only see PrismAIO success, but also **required** to receive PayPal checkout links.
    

Step 1:

*   Create your own Slack Workspace by clicking the "+ - Add workspaces" Icon the left-hand side of your slack application
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F227730734%2Fa94f7f019daaf721b085a381%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1199fff1&sv=2)

Step 2:

*   Once you have created your new workspace, you should be on the homepage for the workspace in your internet browser.
    
*   Scroll to the bottom and locate the `+ Add Applications` button.
    
*   Locate the application `incoming Webhooks` and add it to your workspace
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F227737728%2F667215dadea70c5a80a9ce38%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b3fec4b&sv=2)

Step 3:

*   Once the application has been added, click on the application and go to the settings tab to edit your configuration.
    
*   Pick a channel that the app will post to, then click **Authorize.**
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F227738749%2Fe502693c8543cff8171b609b%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9e0cd1be&sv=2)

Step 4:

*   You can finally click generate in the Webhook URL box to generate your Slack webhook link.
    

#### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/settings#checkout-sound)

Checkout Sound

*   The checkout sound is played on each successful checkout. A custom sound can be imported if in proper MP3 format.
    

#### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/settings#id-3rd-party-integrations)

3rd Party Integrations

Info

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/settings#tab-info-1)

Hue

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/settings#tab-hue)

Nanoleaf

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/settings#tab-nanoleaf)

Phillips Hue and Nanoleaf integration allows PrismAIO users to sync their Phillips Hue and Nanoleaf lighting systems to PrismAIO. Every time you successfully checkout, your lights will flash green. Any time you get a failure, the lights will flash red.

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/settings#setup)

Setup

In order to set up the Phillips Hue Integration, you must first have the following items:

1.) Phillips Hue Enabled Lights

2) Phillips Hue Bridge

To get started, go to the settings -> general -> then locate the Phillips Hue button.

Once selected the following window will pop up.

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F230979204%2F3278fce4912d596d54d9dcf1%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d80a563b&sv=2)

Make sure your Phillips Hue Bridge is next to you and then press the connect button.

Next, press the sync button on your Phillips Hue Bridge. If successful, the Hue button should change colors. We recommend you restart PrismAIO after pairing to ensure that you were successful in the pairing.

Please note that this will only work when your Phillips Hue Bridge is on the same wifi network as the device you are running PrismAIO on.

**If you are having trouble pairing, please check this list for troubleshooting options:**

*   Try repeating the pairing process
    
*   Make sure Hue Bridge is on
    
*   Disconnect from any VPN or proxy from the device you are trying to pair to.
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/settings#setup-1)

Setup

In order to set up the Nanoleaf Integration, you must first find the IP address of your Nanoleaf system by going into your router administrator dashboard/settings.

Each internet provider might have a different way to access the administrator dashboard for their router so please refer to your router's guide. Here is a basic tutorial [video as an example.](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=UZAMTmBq4dA)

Once you have identified the IP address of your Nanoleaf system, you are now ready to turn your Nanoleaf system into pairing mode. To do this, follow the instructions below:

`1) Press and hold down the Effect Select and Power buttons on the controller for about 10 seconds, until the LED on the controller begins flashing.` `2)Release the two buttons and the LED on the controller will remain on and steady`

Next, click on the Nanoleaf button in the settings tab. Then type in the IP address of your Nanoleaf system that we found earlier. The pairing and connect process should be done relatively close to each other in timing. If successfully paired, the Nanoleaf button should change colors. We recommend you restart PrismAIO after pairing to ensure that you were successful in the pairing.

Please note that this will only work when your Nanoleaf is on the same Wi-Fi network as the device you are running PrismAIO on.

**If you are having trouble pairing, please check this list for troubleshooting options:**

*   Try repeating the pairing process
    
*   Make sure you have the correct IP address of your Nanoleaf system.
    
*   Disconnect from any VPN or proxy from the device you are trying to pair to.
    

#### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/settings#app-data)

App Data

*   App data can be imported + exported. This will import or export all of your bot settings.
    
*   To import or export, click the corresponding button.
    

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/settings#site-options)

Site Options


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Site options, also known as your quick task/default settings, are used for quick tasks and are partially used for Automations.
    
    *   To configure global defaults, fill out all of the information under `Configure Global Defaults` and click save.
        
    *   To configure site-specific defaults, first select a site at the top to configure defaults for that specific site.
        
    

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/settings#size-groups)

Size Groups


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Size groups can be used to speed up task creation. They allow you to select multiple sizes and group them together.
    
*   To create a group, name your group and click the sizes you want and click create.
    

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/settings#shipping-rates)

Shipping Rates


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Shipping rates are used to speed up Shopify checkout process but are **not** required.
    
*   To add a rate, click `Create` and name input the shipping rate or input product URL
    
    *   If using `Input Rate`, simply copy the shipping rate and paste it in the shipping rate box.
        
    *   If using `Input Product URL`, select a profile that will be used to grab the rate and use a product URL that is for a product similar in size and weight to the item you will be using the rate for.
        
    

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/settings#accounts)

Accounts


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Accounts are required for sites like Undefeated and optional for sites like Foot Locker.
    
*   To add an account, click `Add`. Next, choose the site you want to add accounts for and paste the email into the `Login` section and password into the `Password` section.
    

To mass input accounts, click `Mass Input`and paste your accounts in the following format: `Login:password` `Login:password` `Login:password`

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/settings#imap)

IMAP


---------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   IMAP is used to automatically grab codes from your email(s) and submit them on sites like Yeezy Supply.
    
*   IMAP is best utilized if you are using a catchall or emails that forward to one primary email. If they do not go to one or a handful primary emails, you will have to sign in to every profile email under the IMAP section which is a lot of work.
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/settings#adding-an-email)

Adding an Email

*   To add an email and sign in, first ensure your email is setup properly via the tabs below.
    

Start

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/settings#tab-start)

Gmail

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/settings#tab-gmail)

Yahoo

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/settings#tab-yahoo)

AOL

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/settings#tab-aol)

Outlook

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/settings#tab-outlook)

*   Click the corresponding tab for proper email setup
    

*   **YOU MUST HAVE 2FA ENABLED**
    

**Enable IMAP**

1.  Open Gmail - [https://mail.google.com/](https://mail.google.com/)
    
2.  Click Settings -> See all settings
    
3.  Click on **POP/IMAP**
    
4.  Scroll down to **IMAP Access**
    
5.  Enable IMAP
    
6.  Click **Save Changes**
    

#### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/settings#create-app-password)

Create App Password

1.  Go to [https://myaccount.google.com/security](https://myaccount.google.com/security)
    
2.  Scroll down to App Passwords and click it
    
3.  Create an app password using the **Other category**
    

Go to [https://login.yahoo.com/myaccount/security](https://login.yahoo.com/myaccount/security)

1.  Scroll down to **Other ways to sign in**
    
2.  Click on **Generate app password** and generate a new app password (Note: Keep this saved somewhere and don’t share it as it will allow us to access your emails through IMAP. If compromised, please delete and create a new IMAP Login in Prism)
    
3.  Use your newly generated _App Password_ to add a new Yahoo account on Prism's IMAP tab.
    

1.  Go to [https://login.aol.com/myaccount/security/](https://login.aol.com/myaccount/security/)
    
2.  Scroll down to **Other ways to sign in**
    
3.  Click on **Generate app password** and generate a new app password (Note: Keep this saved somewhere and don’t share it as it will allow us to access your emails through IMAP. If compromised, please delete and create a new IMAP Login in Refract)
    
4.  Use your newly generated _App Password_ to add a new Yahoo account on Prism's IMAP tab
    

Outlook is not currently supported. You will need to forward your Outlook email to one of the other providers.

*   After you have properly setup your emails, click `Add` and choose the platform that your email uses. After that, add your username/email and password. Finally, click `Create Login` and you are all setup.

# Hibbett | PrismAIO

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/hibbett#task-creation)

Task Creation


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Before creating tasks, you must create a new task group for Hibbett. For help on creating a new task group, follow [this guide.](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/task-creation)
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/hibbett#monitor-setup)

Monitor Setup

*   After creating a task group, you will want to use the product PID provided by our release guides or a third-party. Using a direct link **will not** work. The PID consists of the product SKU and color ID. For example:
    
    *   `https://www.hibbett.com/jordan-1-retro-high-og-white-black-light-smoke-grey-mens-shoe/Q0936.html?dwvar_Q0936_color=1225`
        
        *   The PID (monitor input) for this link would be `Q0936,1225`
            
        
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/hibbett#task-creation-1)

Task Creation

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/hibbett#undefined)

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252Fuploads%252FtfnDjarIQYhdInVNHAvx%252FScreenshot%25202023-03-13%2520at%25207.28.13%2520AM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D69c37ce0-be8a-4060-b95d-84133b593dd3&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2e14abd9&sv=2)

Required Fields

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/hibbett#tab-required-fields)

Optional Fields

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/hibbett#tab-optional-fields)

*   **Profiles:** choose your profiles/profile group
    
*   **Delay:** task delay. Recommended to be left at `3500` and drop the delay at drop time
    
*   **Proxy List:** proxy list used to checkout (leave blank for localhost)
    
*   **Sizes:** the sizes you want the tasks to go for
    
*   **Mode:** cloud vs. restock mode
    
*   **Minutes to submit order at (Restock mode only):** The exact time you want taks to spam order at. I.e for 9:30 put `30` and have your tasks started before then.
    
*   **Second to submit order at (Restock mode only):** The exact second you want taks to spam order at. I.e for 9:30:15 put `15` and have your tasks started before then.
    

*   N/A
    

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/hibbett#restock-vs.-cloud-mode)

Restock vs. Cloud Mode


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Cloud** - Most common and simplest mode, best to use this. It waits until "cloud monitor" finds product and then will try to submit order
    
*   **Restock** - Only sometimes unlocked if a good product restocking at 9:30AM EST - Submits order at the exact minute + second you choose so doesn't have to wait for cloud.
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/hibbett#cloud-monitoring)

Cloud Monitoring

*   If cloud mode I selected, tasks will utilize cloud monitoring. Instead of showing a timer, tasks will say "Waiting for Restock" and are waiting for the cloud monitor to ping and tell tasks to spam payment.
    

Note: tasks must be started before the cloud ping goes off.

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/hibbett#multi-sku-monitoring)

Multi-SKU Monitoring


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   To enable multi-sku, in the task group click the three dots in the task group to enable multi-sku.
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252Fuploads%252FCszt3KRzVBw4xKWrVW0S%252FScreenshot%25202023-03-13%2520at%25207.38.23%2520AM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcd7f462a-c596-4635-a5dd-55e914109b25&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5751647b&sv=2)![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252Fuploads%252FmDOssNXFdmeettVIPRsR%252FScreenshot%25202023-03-13%2520at%25207.36.53%2520AM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc486ea29-18c6-4230-82a8-35e583c9a947&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1a6a39c8&sv=2)

*   Notes about multi-sku:
    
    *   Multi-SKU is slightly slower in terms of flow (has to ATC when something pings via cloud monitoring)
        
    *   Single SKU preloads the item you want (SLIGHTLY faster)
        
    *   Multi-SKU can only run cloud
        
    

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/hibbett#faq)

FAQ


----------------------------------------------------------------

When do I start tasks?

*   Start tasks when CloudFlare is enabled. We will announce in the discord when Cloudflare is enabled.
    

Delays:

*   Monitor: 3500
    
*   Task: 3500
    

How do I know if CloudFlare is enabled?

*   If you navigate to Hibbett on a new Chrome user and see the image below, CloudFlare is enabled.
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F355335755%2Fefbcc501456c3c905a89c10d%2FHibbett%2BCF.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b550a804&sv=2)

What does "Failed to solve CF" mean?

*   If you see this status, restart tasks. It means it was unable to solve the CloudFlare challenge. That is the same thing as being stuck on this step if you were to go manually:
    

Does Hibbett cancel?

*   Typically Hibbett does not cancel but if they suspect you of reselling, they will ban your address.
    

What type of proxies should I run?

*   Residential proxies are required.
    

Do I have to solve captchas?

*   No. There are no captchas that you have to solve. Prism solves all the captchas by itself.
    

Why are my tasks stuck on "Solving PX Captcha"?

*   Tasks that are stuck on solving px captcha mean that the proxies you are using are banned and are not able to pass solving px captcha. The only way to fix this is to use new proxies.
    

When does Hibbett restock?

*   Hibbett restocks on a very consistent pattern. Typically, Hibbett restocks at :15, :17, :35, :37 or in 30 minute increments from those listed times. Another way to see what item is restocking is through the public checkout logger.
    

[PreviousYeezy Supply](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/yeezy-supply)
[NextHibbett Restock Guide](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/hibbett/hibbett-restock-guide)

Last updated 2 years ago

Was this helpful?

# Shopify | PrismAIO

*   Shopify is one of the most common sites to bot as there are numerous sites that drop. PrismAIO supports every Shopify store.
    

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify#task-creation)

Task Creation


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Before creating tasks, you must create a new task group for the Shopify store you want to run on. For help on creating a new task group, follow [this guide.](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/task-creation)
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify#monitor-setup)

Monitor Setup

*   After creating a task group, you will want to decide which monitor input you want to run. Shopify supports keywords (and keyword groups), direct links, and variants. For more information on each one, follow [this guide.](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/task-creation#monitor-inputs)
    

Keywords

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify#tab-keywords)

Keyword Groups

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify#tab-keyword-groups)

Direct Link

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify#tab-direct-link)

Variants

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify#tab-variants)

*   Keywords follow this format: `+key,+word`
    
*   Negative keywords can be added by using a `-` sign. For example: `+key,+word,-bot`. In this case the bot will not pickup any item containing key, word, AND bot.
    

*   Multiple keyword groups can be setup by using parentheses. For example: `(+key)(+word)`. In this case, the bot will pickup any product that contains key OR word.
    

*   A direct link can be used by pasting it directly into the monitor input. For example, if you wanted to run [https://kith.com/products/kh9368-104](https://kith.com/products/kh9368-104)
    , you would add the entire link to a task group for the site Kith.
    

*   Variants can be used by toggling the variants toggle. This can be done by accessing the task group settings (the three dots) and clicking `"Toggle Variants"` There you can add one or multiple variants (which need to be separated and be on their own line). When you have you variants added, you will notice that when you create a task it will allow you to choose one variant or use all the variants.
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify#captcha-settings)

Captcha Settings

*   For Shopify, you **must** use default harvesters. Depends on the site dropping, you will want to have checkpoint, checkout, or both harvesters open.
    

When creating a Shopify harvester, you cannot add a proxy because the harvester will automatically use the task proxy when a captcha is needed (required to pass anti-bot)

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify#enabling-variants)

Enabling Variants

*   If using variants, they must be enabled prior to creating tasks. To enable variants, navigate to task group settings by clicking the three dots next to the monitor status and click `Toggle Variants`
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252F-MkT2zyLQKWJwY9PQcOc%252F-MkT4X1fjci-2oHsZ1e8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daae9c7e6-48be-4231-b40f-2104dafe1468&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d5bc105f&sv=2)

*   Run variants only if the product is not loaded. If the product is already loaded, simply run just the URL.
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify#mode)

Mode

Info

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify#tab-info)

Safe Preload

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify#tab-safe-preload)

Fast

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify#tab-fast)

Safe

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify#tab-safe)

*   Shopify checkout modes are used in order to help increase success on specific site. PrismAIO currently supports 5 checkout modes:
    
    *   Fast (fastest for non-bot protection drops, does **not** preload)
        
    *   Safe (fastest for random bot protection drops and restocks, does **not** preload)
        
    *   Safe Preload (required for scheduled bot protection drops and restocks, does preload)
        
    *   Safe Restock (slowest to initialize, best used on bot-protection drops and restocks with variants and checkpoint goes up before product is released, does preload)
        
    *   Restock (slowest to initialize, best used on non-bot protection drops and restocks with variants, does preload)
        
    

*   Safe Preload is best utilized on sites that drop products **with bot protection and drop time is known** (such as initial drops or scheduled restocks like Kith) OR on restocks.
    
*   Safe Preload will preload a checkout session to skip queue come drop time.
    
*   **Safe Preload is what you should be running 99% of the time! Use it in automations!**
    

*   Fast mode is best utilized on sites that drop products **without** bot protection. In order to get the most out of fast mode, it is best to run with variants for the product or with a direct link. Fast mode is the fastest mode for shopify.
    

*   Safe mode is best utilized on sites that drop products **with bot protection.** Safe mode is designed to pass Shopify bot protection while acting like a "human". Safe mode will **NOT PRELOAD** a checkout session to ship queue. Best used on sites with a password page or for use with random restocks that use checkpoint/bot protection.
    

Safe Version Use Cases:

*   Safe (use when checkpoint **AND** product load at the same time)
    
*   Safe Preload (use when checkpoint **AND** product load at the same time for a **SCHEDULED DROP)**
    
    *   **Use for restocks!**
        
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify#task-creation-1)

Task Creation

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252F-MkTRP2zCstpXOpdbNU_%252F-MkTRrdXoU-p1jVeqnfy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D20d0eae9-ee85-4c09-b6ef-99f501147d5f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d714d1d&sv=2)

Required Fields

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify#tab-required-fields)

Optional Fields

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify#tab-optional-fields)

*   **Profiles:** choose your profiles/profile group
    
*   **Delay:** task delay. Recommended to be left at `3500` and drop the delay at drop time
    
*   **Proxy List:** proxy list used to checkout (leave blank for localhost)
    
*   **Size:** size(s) the task will go for. If selecting multiple sizes, it will go for any size in your range
    
*   **Mode:** mode the task will use to checkout
    

*   **Accounts:** account the task will log in to before checking out
    
*   **Shipping rate:** shipping rate the bot may use to speed up the checkout process
    

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify#faq)

FAQ


----------------------------------------------------------------

What is Shopify bot protection?

*   Shopify's bot protection often consists of a checkpoint captcha, checkout captcha, and requiring the user to run a safe mode when checking out. Sometimes they will enable proxy throttling which will effect a lot of proxies ability to add to cart and checkout.
    

Does Shopify cancel?

*   Many shopify sites are very strict on orders with sites like Kith being the most strict. It does vary from site to site though.
    

What type of proxies should I run?

*   ISP are recommended as they have the highest chance of passing proxy protection.
    

Does AYCD/2Cap/CapMonster/Anti-Cap work for Shopify?

*   Yes. They may be slower than solving manually but are best utilized on restocks.
    

What does "Payment Failure" mean?

*   Payment failures can mean that your card was declined but I doesn't always mean that. It can also mean the checkout was blocked by the site because of the bot, captcha score, or one attempted checkout per credit card at the same time on some sites.
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify#h_19a7c1be78)

**Custom Shopify**

How to setup a custom site?

*   A custom site can be setup by clicking the `"Custom Site (Shopify)"` button which can be found when creating a task group. From there you will need to add the host URL. The host url is the main page for the site. For example, if you wanted to add [https://www.prismaio.com/dashboard](https://www.prismaio.com/dashboard)
    , the host URL would be [https://www.prismaio.com](https://www.prismaio.com/dashboard)
    .
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1545556644-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-Mjpf0oK2XC20C94VPcj%252F-MkT2zyLQKWJwY9PQcOc%252F-MkT5A1_TQ73vP_jX-XY%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De8d864c3-3a60-4a04-ac2b-906da763ab3b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d8ba3501&sv=2)

How do I use accounts on custom Shopify?

*   This can be done by first creating a task group for the custom shopify site. After that has been created, you can then go to the accounts tab in the settings tab of the bot and add your accounts there.

[NextSite Specific Setup](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup)

# Site Specific Setup | PrismAIO

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#a-ma-maniere)

A Ma Maniere


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Info

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#tab-info)

Setup

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#tab-setup)

*   A Ma Maniere/APB Store/Social Status typically release at 10AM EST. They typically do a raffle first and drop leftovers online.
    

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#monitor-info)

**Monitor Info**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Use `keywords`. Make sure you have the proper negative keywords too as they have a bunch of products on their site and you don't want to pickup the wrong product.
    

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#task-creation)

**Task Creation**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#h_ab78b1264f)

Delays

*   Monitor: Start tasks at `8000+`, drop tasks to `2500` **15 seconds** before the release
    
*   Task: Keep at `2500` for the entire duration of the drop
    

####

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#eric-emanuel)

Eric Emanuel


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Info

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#tab-info-8)

Setup

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#tab-setup-8)

*   Eric Emanuel releases hype shorts on a pretty consistent basis. They always release at 12PM EST.
    

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#monitor-info-8)

**Monitor Info**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Use `keywords`. They **do not** include the color of the short in the product title so running keywords will pickup any color of short. To run a specific color, the recommended setup is to use fake keywords like `(+prism-is-the-goat)` and **mass link change** to the link of the correct item you want. The easiest way to do this would be to open the in-bot monitor and click the paper-clip icon to copy the link of the correct item.
    

![](https://help.prismaio.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F369785754%2Fdf8a1afa9a8880dae437f84e%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4d2b75ca&sv=2)

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#task-creation-8)

**Task Creation**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#h_33c742843f)

Delays

*   Monitor: Start tasks at `8000+`, drop tasks to `2500` **15 seconds** before the release
    
*   Task: Keep at `2500` for the entire duration of the drop
    

#### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#h_32144ce5de)

Mode

*   Prioritize `Safe` mode
    

#### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#h_fbbae01334)

Accounts

*   `Not required`
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#h_54a750bfab)

**Start Time**

*   Start tasks **3-5 minutes** before the release. If it is a super hyped release, queue may be longer so you would want to start tasks earlier.
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#h_76dd43b8ec)
