---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#h_bfcc86c4e5)

Delays

*   Monitor: Start tasks at `8000+`, drop tasks to `2500` **15 seconds** before the release
    
*   Task: Keep at `2500` for the entire duration of the drop
    

#### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#h_0ec8f42947)

Mode

*   `Safe Preload`
    

#### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#h_8649d1c732)

Accounts

*   `Not required`
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#h_f5187ceb16)

**Start Time**

*   Start tasks **5-10 minutes** before the release. If it is a super hyped release, queue may be longer so you would want to start tasks earlier.
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#h_1fb3392bd1)

**Harvesters**

*   Have multiple **Shopify Checkpoint** harvesters open
    
*   Open one **Shopify Question** harvester in case a question is required
    

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#shoe-palace)

Shoe Palace


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Info

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#tab-info-14)

Setup

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#tab-setup-14)

*   Shoe Palaces releases are supposed to be at 10AM EST, but they typically end up dropping a few minutes before that. They will load checkpoint before they release the shoes, typically at 10:55 AM EST, so start solving as many checkpoint captchas as you can.
    

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#monitor-info-14)

**Monitor Info**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Use product URL
    

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#task-creation-14)

**Task Creation**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#h_09f22ca6fe)

Delays

*   Monitor: Start tasks at `8000+`, drop monitor to `2500` **15 seconds** before the release
    
*   Task: Run with **HIGH** task before dropk, and drop to `2500` 15 seconds before drop. Best to use auto delay drop!
    

#### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#h_39ae9fa126)

Mode

*   `Safe Preload`
    

#### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#h_e9c63bdc72)

Accounts

*   `Not required`
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#h_4a1ba530d8)

**Start Time**

*   Start tasks **7-9 minutes** before the release. If it is a super hyped release, queue may be longer so you would want to start tasks earlier.
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#h_731921c874)

**Harvesters**

*   Have multiple **Shopify Checkpoint** harvesters open
    

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#shop-nice-kicks)

Shop Nice Kicks

Setup

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#tab-setup-15)

*   Shop Nice Kicks releases are supposed to be at 10AM EST, but they typically end up dropping 2 to 5 minutes after that. They will load checkpoint before they release the shoes so start solving as many checkpoint captchas as you can.
    

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#monitor-info-15)

*   Task: Run with **HIGH** task before dropk, and drop to `2500` 15 seconds before drop. Best to use auto delay drop!

Social Status

Setup

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#tab-setup-16)

*   A Ma Maniere/APB Store/Social Status typically release at 10AM EST. They typically do a raffle first and drop leftovers online.
    

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#monitor-info-16)

**Monitor Info**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Use `keywords`. Make sure you have the proper negative keywords too as they have a bunch of products on their site and you don't want to pickup the wrong product.

Shipping Rate

###

**Start Time**

*   Start tasks **3-8 minutes** before the release. If it is a super hyped release, queue may be longer so you would want to start tasks earlier.
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#h_3f675746c5)

**Harvesters**

*   Have multiple **Shopify Checkpoint** harvesters open
    

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#undefeated)

Undefeated


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Info

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#tab-info-18)

Setup

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#tab-setup-18)

*   Undefeated releases are typically at 8AM EST. Sometimes they will drop at a different time which is typically announced via their Instagram
    

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#monitor-info-18)

**Monitor Info**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Prioritize `keywords` and be ready to mass link change
    

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#task-creation-18)

**Task Creation**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#h_075ab3772f)

Delays

*   Monitor: Start tasks at `8000+`, drop tasks to `2500` **15 seconds** before the release
    
*   Task: Keep at `2500` for the entire duration of the drop
    

#### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#h_d40c1f033b)

Mode

*   `Safe Preload`
    

#### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#h_713484e834)

Accounts

*   `Required`
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#h_ba971bb9cb)

**Start Time**

*   Start tasks **5-10 minutes** before the release. If it is a super hyped release, queue may be longer so you would want to start tasks earlier.
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#h_fbe493bda4)

**Harvesters**

*   Have multiple **Shopify Checkpoint** harvesters open, with 1-2 **Shopify Checkout** harvesters open.
    

### 

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/shopify/site-specific-setup#h_7fe4ef4af8)

**Restocks**

*   Throughout the release day, Undefeated may restock the product **WITHOUT** bot protection so be sure to setup [Automations](https://help.prismaio.com/en/?q=automations)
     and [quick task](https://help.prismaio.com/en/articles/4102527-how-to-set-up-quick-task-settings)
     defaults.

# Footsites (USA) Automation SKU List | PrismAIO

[](https://help.prismaio.com/module-guides/footsites-north-america/automation-sku-list#automation-guides)

Automation Guides:


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [General Guide](https://help.prismaio.com/tasks-and-task-groups/automations)
    

Below are suggested products that were profitable at the time they were added. As with all markets, prices change constantly so be sure to only add products to your automation list that you are comfortable running.
